et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;  
And two cauteries between the fifth and sixth ribs, slightly declining toward the back.  

et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;  
And one cautery in the middle of the chest, another above the stomach, one between the two shoulders, and two on the sides of the chest near the cautery between the shoulders.  

et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.  
And do not press your hand, but act gently, as if inhaling a scent.  

Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;  
Some ancients said that some men use a cautery shaped like a razor, heat it, and place it between the ribs until it reaches the abscess.  

et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.  
And the pain escapes, as we have said about the abscess of the liver.  

Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.  
But in this procedure, there is a risk that the patient may die immediately, or a fistula may form that cannot be healed.  

de la mice  
Of the spleen  

Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.  
When you treat the disease of the spleen as we have explained in the divisions of treatments, and it does not help, then there are three methods of cautery, all of which are good.  

Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;  
One of these methods is to make three cauteries, or four, in a line along the length of the spleen, following the shape of the cautery for the liver that we described earlier.  

et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;  
And do not press your hand with the cautery, and let the patient often lie on his back.  

et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;  
Another method of cautery is to heat the cautery with two prongs, as we have shown for the dislocation of the shoulder.  

et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.  
And lift the part near the spleen where the patient’s pain occurs on the left side, and let the elevation with which you lift the part follow the alignment of the body, and the cautery should be placed across the width of the body.  

Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.  
Then insert the two heated prongs until the part is pierced through to the other side, and then remove the cautery; in this way, there will be four cauteries.  

Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.  
And if you wish, cauterize with the cautery that has three prongs.  

Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.  
Afterward, treat it when it has expelled the corruption over time, and this is often more effective than the other treatments previously mentioned.  

de ydropisie  
Of dropsy  

Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».  
Cautery is not useful for dropsy, except in the method called "ascites."  

Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;  
When you treat it according to the methods we have described in the divisions, and your treatment does not work, then you must make four cauteries around the belly, one above the stomach, one above the liver, one above the spleen, two on the back along the spine, and one near the chest.  

et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.  
And let the cauteries be placed close to the thickness of the heart.  

Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;  
Afterward, leave the cautery open to expel corruption over time, and do not neglect the treatment of the patient after the cautery.  

et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.  
And the healing will hasten, and the two intentions will align with the help of God.  

Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;  
The form of the cautery for the belly should be the pointed one we described earlier.  

et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.  
And the one for the back should be oval-shaped, as mentioned earlier.  

de l’enfleure des piez  
On the swelling of the feet  

Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;  
When the feet are swollen in one who is dropsical and full of citrine water, you must cauterize the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring toe;  

et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.  
and lift your hand with the cautery without twisting.  

Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:  
And do not go too deeply, so the citrine water may flow out, and let the cauterization follow this form:  

Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;  
Then make two cauterizations on each leg at the tip of the calf muscle;  

et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;  
and let the cauterizations be long, one below the knee in front and the other behind, in the middle of the leg;  

et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;  
and leave the cauterizations open for a long time without cleaning, so that the water may flow out;  

aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.  
then proceed with the other treatments we have described.  

de la menoison  
On diarrhea  

Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;  
When diarrhea arises from cold and moisture, so that the retentive and digestive power of the stomach and intestines is weakened, and it cannot be cured by ordinary treatments;  

et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;  
and you see the patient enduring well and of strong constitution, then make a large cauterization on the stomach according to what has been previously discussed about stomach cauterization, in a circular form;  

et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.  
and four small cauterizations around the navel with a fine pointed cautery, and two cauterizations on the hips.  

Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.  
And if you see abundant moisture and the patient enduring, then make a cauterization on the wrist, one on each shoulder blade, and two small cauterizations on the stomach beside the large one, for the treatment is effective when there is good support.  

de la cure des emorroydes  
On the treatment of hemorrhoids  

Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:  
When hemorrhoids are in the anus, whether one or more, and are chronic and made of thick, cold, and corrupted moist humors, and treatments as we have described in sections do not help, then make cauterizations:  

III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;  
Three on the spine, at the outermost part just below the nape of the neck, arranged triangularly, and one below the navel by two fingers' breadth;  

et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;  
and if you think their stomach is cold, and the food does not digest, and the face appears swollen, then make one large cauterization on the stomach as previously described, another on the liver, and another on the spleen with the fine-pointed cautery;  

et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.  
and leave the cauterization open for a long time.  

Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then treat the area until it is healed.  

de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»  
On the fleshiness called "thelul"  

Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;  
When you cut the thelul, heat the cautery shaped like a razor, and then place it fully heated upon the cut thelul;  

et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;  
and keep your hand there until the cautery reaches the root of the vein from which the blood flows;  

fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;  
do this once or twice, and if there are many theluls, cauterize each one as we have described;  

aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;  
then treat with beneficial ointments until they are healed;  

et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.  
and if you cauterize with a large cautery on the alchatim, it will be more effective.  

de plaie mal curee  
On poorly healed wounds  

Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.  
When the patient cannot endure incisions or openings, as we will describe in its section, such a condition arises that it cannot be healed except by cautery.  

Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.  
When someone has a fistula, and it is old and emits putrefaction and corrupted moisture, you must probe it with a fine tent and ascertain with the tent how deep it is.  

Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;  
Then heat a cautery that resembles a razor, and insert it into the fistula to the depth indicated by the tent, and repeat the cauterization until the rotten and corrupted tissue is burned away, once, twice, or three times, depending on the need;  

et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.  
and take care not to burn the nerves that are there, nor the large veins.  

se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;  
If the fistula leads to the bladder or intestine, take care in those areas, and only perform this in fleshy parts, ensuring it does not penetrate.  

aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;  
Then treat the area until it is healed, and if the wound has closed and the matter has been removed for a long time, know that the area is fully healed;  

et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;  
but if the matter has not been removed, know that the area is hollowed and the bone at the base is corrupted;  

et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.  
and thus as one of these cases we will describe in its section.  

de la maladie des reins  
On kidney disease  

Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;  
When pain from cold occurs in the kidneys, accompanied by large winds, and there is no desire for women, then you must cauterize the kidneys on both sides with the fine-pointed cautery we mentioned earlier;  

et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.  
and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in a line, which will provide greater relief.  

de la vessie  
On the bladder  

Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;  
When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, make a cauterization on the upper part of the bladder, where the pubic hair begins, one on the right and one on the left, each as long as a thumb joint;  

et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;  
and make one cauterization on the back, or two if needed;  

et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.  
and let the cauterization be fine-pointed, as previously described.  

de la marris  
On the uterus  

Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;  
When the uterus is cold and moist, preventing conception, and the menstrual flow is corrupted and delayed;  

et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:  
and when they come, great pain is felt:  

adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;  
then three cauterizations must be made around the navel, as we have described for bladder cauterization, and two cauterizations on the back;  

et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.  
and let the cauterization be fine-pointed, as we have described.  

de la hainche  
On the hip  

Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;  
When viscous moisture descends to the socket of the hip, causing it to shift from its place, and the sign is that one thigh is longer than the other when measured together;  

et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;  
and the separation point is found to be hollow, then you must cauterize the patient on the socket of the hip with a circular cauterization, bleeding the area around the socket as it turns, so that the socket is enclosed within the circle;  

et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.  
and let the cautery be of the type used for the stomach.  

Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;  
And if this cautery is not available, make three large olive-shaped cauterizations, as deep as the entire core;  

et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and treat the area until it is healed.  

de la dolor de la hainche  
On hip pain  

Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:  
When pain occurs in the hip socket from cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated as described in the section but the treatment does not work, and the condition is chronic:  

adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.  
then you must purge the patient of thick humors with fetid pills or other suitable pills.  

Aprés li fai cautere;  
Then perform cauterization;  

et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:  
and the method of cauterization follows two approaches:  

c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.  
namely, the use of burning medicines and fire cautery.  

Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:  
Fire cauterization has many methods, one of which is as follows:  

que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;  
that you make three triangular cauterizations on the hip socket in this shape, with good depth and size, spacing each cauterization by the width of a finger, and using an olive-shaped cautery;  

aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:  
sometimes a cauterization is made in the center on the top of the hip, resulting in four cauterizations in this pattern:  

Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;  
And if you wish, cauterize with the circular cautery we mentioned earlier for hip dislocation;  

mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.  
but do so in a way that the circle encompasses the entire hip, and all the thickness of the core is burned.  

Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.  
This is the method used in sciatica when the pain is in the hip and does not extend to the thigh or leg.  

Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;  
And if it extends to the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations where the patient says the pain is, and one cauterization above the ankle by four fingers' breadth, slightly to the left;  

et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;  
and let the cautery be knife-shaped, burning to the core's thickness;  

et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».  
and if the patient feels the pain extending to the toes or nearby, cauterize where the pain is felt, making three or four points with the cautery called "points."  

Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;  
And if necessary, make more cauterizations;  

et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.  
and if the pain is below the knee toward the thigh, make a cauterization with the knife-shaped or circular cautery, and take great care in all your cauterizations not to leave the cautery so long that you burn the nerves and large arteries, or cause the patient greater harm and contraction.  

Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.  
And I myself have seen many who applied cautery on the ankle of the foot, and left it so long that the leg became completely swollen, as well as the foot, and the entire foot was pierced and corrupted.  

Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.  
After a loosening of the belly from which he died.  

Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.  
And if the pain is in two places together, apply cautery to both, in this manner.  

Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;  
And the wise said concerning the cautery of the hip, for which this is the method, make such an iron, and let its head be as thick as a small date, or a little less, and let it have serrations, and let the distance between one serration and the next be the size of a thumb’s joint.  

et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;  
And let the serrations be open on two sides, and let them resemble knots, and let there be a well-made iron handle.  

et c’est li forme:  
And this is the shape:  

Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;  
And let it be heated until it is completely red and sparks fly from it, and then place it on the hipbone of the afflicted side, and let it be turned on the sound side.  

et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;  
And cauterize it once with a round cautery and leave it for three days.  

et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;  
And then make a plaster of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time.  

aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Afterwards, treat it with ointments until it is healed.  

Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;  
Albucasis says that we use this cautery little because of the fear of its appearance, and we see few who use it.  

et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.  
And yet it is one of the good cauteries, for those who can endure it, and in the cases where it is appropriate.  

Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;  
The cautery of burning medicine is such that you make a serrated instrument on which the edge of the opening descends, and let it be made of bronze or iron with a long surface, and let there be two knobs in its height, and between each the thickness of a finger.  

et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:  
And let them be open on the outside and above, and joined together in this form:  

Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;  
Then place it on the hipbone of the patient lying on their healthy side, and press your hand firmly on the hipbone.  

aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.  
Afterwards, pour between the two circles some warm water that has been heated slightly by fire, and leave it for an hour, and let the patient endure its heat and burning.  

Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;  
For they feel a stinging sensation like that of fire.  

et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;  
And when the stinging sensation has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and wash the hip with fresh water, and leave it like this for three days, and apply butter until what is blackened from the scalding is removed.  

et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;  
And leave it for three days so that the rotting may be expelled.  

et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.  
And this would be the final aid after treatment with ointments until it is healed.  

Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;  
And if the pain has extended to the thigh or to the leg, make an instrument to hold water in the same manner as you did for the hip.  

et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.  
And this is the method of hot water, and I have written about it in the treatise on the rectification of medicine.  

Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.  
Take alkali and quicklime, equal parts of each, and grind them together, and place them in a new pot.  

ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;  
In which there is a small opening outside, just large enough for the tip of a razor to enter.  

et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;  
And place over this pot another well-sealed pot, and pour over the alkali and lime some fresh water until there is a finger’s width above the powders when you press it with your hand.  

et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.  
And leave it like this until some distilled water descends and collects in the sealed pot, then take all this water and pour it over the lime and alkali as before.  

Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.  
And then it will be very strong water and is used in many medical operations and in the cauterization of other body parts.  

Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.  
For it acts in the same way as fire, and there are also other medicines with which one can effectively cauterize the hip, such as resin, honey, anacardium, lime, and soap, all mixed together.  

Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.  
And Galen tells us of a cure in which a man was healed of hip pain and sciatica, and he praises it greatly, saying that no other treatment was done, and that he was healed in a single session when this treatment was applied, and he bathed as instructed below.  

Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;  
And he says in this manner that you take fresh and dry green litharge, grind it well with a bit of grease, and apply it to the hip, the thigh, and the leg where the pain is, and bind it.  

et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.  
And leave it for three hours, or until the patient no longer feels the burning.  

Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.  
And then make him enter the bath until his body is slightly soaked, and then put him to bed, and the pain will leave entirely, and he will be healed.  

Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.  
And know that no one should use cautery with such medicines unless it is after cleansing the body.  

Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;  
And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat dung, it helps greatly.  

et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.  
And the cautery should be done in this way.  

Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.  
Take wool and soak it in old oil, and place it on the hollow between the big toe and the next toe, which is called the fossa.  

Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;  
Then take dry goat dung, burn it until it becomes charcoal, place it on the wool, and leave it until it is extinguished.  

et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;  
And repeat this again, and do not stop until you judge that it reaches the hip and the pain has ceased.  

et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».  
And this type of cautery is called the "goat cautery."  

de la dolor dou dos  
On back pain  

Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.  
When pain occurs in the back, whether from a fall, a blow, excessive evacuation, or something resembling the spread of cold matter, cautery is useless in all these cases except for the one caused by the infusion of cold matter.  

Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;  
It is necessary, after the patient has been purged with fetid pills or similar remedies, to make on his back, where the pain is, three lines marked with ink, and on each line, apply five or more cauteries, depending on the strength and capacity of the patient to endure.  

et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;  
And the cautery should be done according to the method called "point cautery."  

et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:  
And if you wish, make three or four cauteries with the medium clavilary cautery, in this form:  

Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;  
This disease often occurs in small children, and the signs at the beginning are that they have labored breathing when they rise, and fear.  

et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.  
And you find in the lower spine of the back and the nodes the swelling that appears above the other vertebrae.  

Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.  
When you see this and want to treat it, cauterize it with the circular cautery in this form.  

Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.  
So that the cautery equally covers each part of the spine.  

Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.  
And if you wish, cauterize around the spine with the pointed cautery in two or three lines, with the points close to one another.  

Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.  
Afterwards, treat the area until it is healed as we have described, and ensure that you do not administer cautery in a hump caused by nerve spasm.  

de la dolor des jointes  
On joint pain  

Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:  
When joint pain is caused by moisture spreading to each part of the body, and when the pain is in the foot, which doctors properly call "podagra," and when it is caused by cold and medicines cannot cure it, it is treated by cautery in this manner:  

fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:  
Make many cauteries around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-shaped, in this form:  

Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».  
And if necessary to touch the surface of the foot, make the cautery with the one called the "point cautery."  

Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;  
And if the pains extend to the knees and other joints, which happens often, apply to each knee three or four cauteries on each side, using the olive-shaped cautery.  

et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.  
And if more are needed, apply more, but do not keep your hand there except until the thickness of the core is burned.  

Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.  
And if the pains descend to the knees and back, apply the cautery as described in the previous chapter.  

Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;  
And if the pains are in the hands, make two lines of points around the wrist;  

et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;  
and if pain remains in the fingers, make points on each joint and on the back of the hand;  

et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.  
and if the pains extend to the elbows or to the shoulders, cauterize each part, manage the patient well, and administer medicines.  

Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.  
For if you provide good management and purge phlegm, he will be healed with God's help.  

de la routure dou syfac  
Of the rupture of the scrotum  

Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;  
When a rupture occurs in the groin, and the bowels descend into the testicles and it is recent, it is necessary that when you intend to treat it, the patient does not eat that day;  

et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;  
and that he consumes things that loosen the bowels, so that the feces descend from his body;  

aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;  
then make him lie on his back between your hands, and instruct him to hold his breath until the bowels are returned to their place, and guide them back with your fingers, and incise at the edge below the rupture above the pubic bone, marking with a shape resembling half a circle over the body;  

puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:  
then heat the cautery tool, which has the following form:  

tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.  
until it is white-hot and emits sparks.  

Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;  
Then return the bowels to their place;  

et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;  
and the assistant holds his hand over them so that they do not return out;  

et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;  
and spread the patient’s thighs well, placing a cushion under him and one assistant on his thighs, and another on his chest to hold his hands;  

puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;  
then place the cautery tool on the marked spot with your whole hand, hold it steady, and keep it there until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat again until you come to the bone;  

et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;  
and be careful that the bowels do not protrude when you apply the cautery;  

que tu ne le brulasses;  
so that you do not burn them;  

et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.  
and so that the patient does not die or suffer other harm.  

Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.  
And know that if you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.  

Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;  
And it is necessary that the cautery for children be fine according to the measure of their bones, and for adults as large as their size requires;  

aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;  
after three days, treat the cautery site with butter until the burn is alleviated;  

aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;  
afterward treat it with other ointments until it is healed, and have the patient lie on his back for forty days until the wound is well closed;  

et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.  
and it is necessary that his diet remain light for a long time, so that the bowels do not protrude when he resumes walking.  

Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;  
And after forty days, when he wishes to get up, provide him with a well-made bandage, and have him wear it for another forty days;  

et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;  
and let him rest well, exert himself little, and avoid excessive consumption of food and drink, as well as loud shouting;  

et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.  
and when he follows this instruction, he will be fully healed.  

Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.  
And I will next discuss the treatment for cutting in its chapter.  

de la routure dou ventre  
Of rupture of the abdomen  

Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;  
When ruptures occur in other parts of the abdomen and are noticeable, and you want them to grow no further, make a round cautery according to its size, and burn one-third of its depth;  

aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;  
then treat it as we have described;  

et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:  
and some of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with a cautery of three angles in this shape:  

mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.  
but first mark the site with ink and draw a line across the width above the rupture, and another below, and place your hand in the middle with the cross-shaped cautery.  

Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.  
But the first cautery is lighter and milder.  

de dolor anciene en aucun membre  
Of chronic pain in any limb  

Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.  
When pain occurs in any limb, either from a fall or a blow, and that pain persists for a long time, and medicinal treatments are ineffective, then it is necessary to cauterize it with a cautery called "point," and the cautery should match the length of the limb, its smallness, its weakness, its strength, and the location of the twisting and the pain.  

s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;  
If he is healed from the first cautery, that is good;  

se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.  
if not, repeat another cautery on the same spot, for such is the practice that it must move to the nearest limb, therefore you must apply cautery until the patient is healed.  

de meselerie  
Of leprosy  

Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.  
Leprosy is sometimes greatly helped by cautery, and particularly the disease that comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.  

Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:  
When you wish to cauterize it, observe whether the disease is at its beginning, and if it is treated as we have described in the section, and it neither worsens nor remains, and you fear that the corruption will take over the entire patient, then apply five cauteries on the head:  

I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;  
One in the middle of the head at the crown, and another toward the forehead at the hairline;  

et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;  
and two on the two temples, and one at the back of the head at the occiput;  

et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;  
and hold your hand there until the cautery reaches the bone, and until the scabs rise outward so that the vapors of the thick humors can escape;  

et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.  
and cauterize on the skin according to what is described above.  

Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;  
And if the leprosy is spread throughout the body;  

et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;  
and it appears clearly, it is necessary to cauterize with the cauteries we described on the head, and one cautery on the tip of the nose, two on the spine of the neck, six on the spine of the back, one large one on the sacrum and another beside it, and two on the two shoulders;  

et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;  
and two on the elbows, two on the tendons of the chest, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the palms;  

et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;  
and be careful of the nerves located in the lower back, that you do not burn them;  

et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.  
and sometimes one cautery is applied on the wrist bone, another on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.  

Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;  
And know that the more cauteries you perform, the more you help him, and many benefit from it;  

et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.  
and know that the patient does not feel the pain of the cautery as the healthy do, because the body is already entirely corrupted.  

Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.  
And it is necessary that the cauteries be large or small according to the limbs and joints, as you will find in the forms of the instruments.  

Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.  
Afterward, treat the site with bean flour mixed with honey and other remedies until it is healed.  

Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;  
When swelling appears in a limb and has been treated with medicines, oils, and plasters, and it is not healed, then apply cauteries to the limb according to the size and smallness of the limb;  

et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;  
and let the cautery penetrate slightly into the thickness of the flesh;  

puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then treat it with ointments until it is healed.  

Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;  
And sometimes a cautery is applied to the hand, the foot, and the back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus the swelling is removed;  

et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.  
and nevertheless no one should undertake this unless he is knowledgeable about the limbs and the paths of the nerves that move the body.  

de albaras  
Of albaras  

Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;  
When the disease called "albaras" is aged, and medicinal remedies are of no use, then cauterize it with a slightly deep cautery, according to the thickness of the flesh, until the whiteness is removed, and its color is changed;  

puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;  
then treat it with flour of beans and lentils mixed with rose oil, plantain leaves, and blood of a dove and a lark, each in equal parts;  

et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and let it all be mixed together, wrapped in a cloth, and applied to the site until it is healed.  

li cure de chancre par cautere  
The treatment of chancre with cautery  

Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.  
When a chancre appears at the beginning, and you wish to stop it, cauterize it with a cautery that resembles a circle, all around the chancre.  

Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;  
And yet the wise men have said that one should also cauterize in the middle of the chancre;  

et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;  
and yet this does not seem good to me, for I fear it might become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen this happen sometimes;  

et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.  
and it is more proper that it be cauterized around, with the cautery called "circle," as we have said for many cauteries.  

de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer  
Of the swelling that cannot mature  

Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;  
When someone has a disease called "adubelati," and it delays in maturing, either because of its excessive production, or because of the age of the patient when he is decrepit (that is to say, too old), and he has little blood, or because of the season;  

et tu la vues haster de meurer:  
and you wish to hasten its maturation:  

adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;  
then cauterize around it with many small cauteries in pricking motions;

aprés le laisse ensi.  
Then leave it like this.  

Car elle se hastera de meureir.  
For it will hasten to die.  

Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:  
And if you want to pierce it with the cautery, then heat the cautery, of which this is the method:  

Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.  
And place your hand in the middle of that ailment which is called "adubelati," until the cautery has pierced the core, and let the cautery be such that the patient feels it externally in such a way that the flow of the corruption is alleviated.  

Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.  
Then treat it until it is completely healed.  

li cure dou feu par fer  
The treatment by fire with iron.  

Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.  
There is another kind of disease which is called "corrodens," and it is nothing other than a consumption of the limb, for it eats the limbs just as fire consumes dry wood.  

Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;  
If you see this disease in a place that can endure cautery together with fire, then heat the pointed cauteries, both small and large, according to what is needed for the location of the disease.  

aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.  
Then cauterize all around so that you remove all the corruption, and let none of it remain, so that everything that is corrupt is removed.  

Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.  
Then leave it for three days, and apply sulfur crushed with oil to the cauterized areas until the burns from the fire are removed, and all the corruption as well.  

Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.  
Then treat it with ointments that generate flesh.  

Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;  
And if you see after three days that healthy flesh is not growing, that is fine;  

et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.  
And if not, then begin the cautery again on what remains of the corrupted areas.  

Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;  
And this condition has sometimes been treated with sharp medicine instead of fire cautery;  

mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:  
but nevertheless fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already explained the treatment with sharp medicine in the section:  

pren la quant tu en as mestier.  
take it when you need it.  

des porrelz qui vienent as piez  
About corns that appear on the feet  

Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.  
Many times it happens that on the feet a condition arises, which we call "clos," and it is a hard lump that injures the foot.  

Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.  
And the cautery for this condition is of two kinds.  

C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.  
That is, fire cautery and hot water cautery.  

Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;  
Fire cautery is when you heat a small cautery tool shaped like the nib of a quill, made of good iron and sized to encompass the corn on all sides, with fine edges;  

aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;  
then place it hot over the corn, and rotate your hand all around the corn until it reaches the base of the corn;  

et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;  
and leave it like this for three days until it starts to discharge pus;  

puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.  
then make a poultice of wild mallows crushed with salt, leave the poultice on all night, and the corn will fall off and be uprooted from its roots.  

Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then treat the area with ointment that generates flesh until it is healed.  

Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et en piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;  
And if they have spread over the body, which often happens on the hands and feet, you should apply hot water cautery there;  

et est en teil maniere:  
and it is done in this way:  

pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;  
take a small tube of brass or iron, or a quill-shaped tool, and place it over the corn or the wart;  

et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;  
place the tube so it surrounds the area, then pour a little hot water inside, hold your hand firmly, and press while rotating so that the edge of the tube reaches the root of the corn and allows the hot water to penetrate deeply to the root;  

et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;  
and have the patient endure the sting of the hot water for a while;  

puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.  
then leave it like this, and it will be uprooted entirely with its roots.  

Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.  
Do this one after another until you remove all those on the body, then treat them with ointments that generate flesh.  

li cure dou trembler  
The treatment for trembling  

Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;  
When someone trembles from nerve coldness, quartan fever, or another cause, you should apply four cauteries on the spine of the back, one cautery between each vertebra;  

et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;  
and one cautery on the foot, and one on the stomach with the olive-shaped cautery;  

si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.  
then the trembling will stop, and the recovery from the cold condition will hasten.  

des pustules puans  
About foul-smelling pustules  

Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.  
Sometimes foul-smelling pustules appear on the body, caused by thick, corrupted matter.  

si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:  
It is necessary, when they first appear, to apply cautery on the head of each pustule:  

un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.  
a fine cautery made of myrtle wood, with its tip heated in fire, or from the root of long birthwort, or a lenticular cautery.  

Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;  
Sometimes they are cauterized at the start when they appear, in this manner, and they cannot grow further, as the excess causing them is interrupted, and they are healed;  

mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.  
but it must be done after bloodletting.  

quant li artere est copee  
When an artery is cut  

Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;  
Many times, there are great flows of blood from an artery cut in a wound that comes outward, or in the incision of an abscess, or in the cauterization of a limb, and similar cases;  

et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.  
and it is a very serious thing to stop.  

Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;  
And yet, when this happens to someone, quickly place your index finger on the wound in the vein and press so firmly that the blood calms under your finger, and no drop escapes;  

puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;  
then heat several olive-shaped cauteries, both small and large, until they are all red-hot;  

puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.  
then take one, large or small depending on the wound and the location where the artery is broken, and place the cautery on that vein where your finger was, and hold it there until the bleeding is stopped.  

Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.  
And if it gushes out when you lift your finger from the vein and the cautery cools, quickly take another of the cauteries from the fire.  

Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;  
And do not stop repeating this one after another until the bleeding is stopped.  

et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;  
And be careful not to burn the nearby nerve, and that no other harm comes to the patient.  

et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:  
And know that when blood flows from an artery, it cannot be properly stopped, especially if the artery is large, except by one of the four methods we have mentioned:  

ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;  
either by cautery, by extraction when it is not drawn out, by strong binding with thread, or by applying medicines that have the power to stop blood.  

et soit liee et estrainte avennament.  
And it should be tied and tightened properly.  

Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.  
Whoever uses methods like tightly binding with cloths, applying burning things, or other similar measures will find they help little or not at all.  

Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;  
And if this happens to someone and there is no doctor or medicine available, they should place their index finger on the vein’s wound as we have said, pressing firmly until the bleeding is stopped over the wound and the vein.  

et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;  
And do not move the finger, but frequently wet it with very cold water until the blood congeals, thickens, and stops.  

et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.  
And from then on, use the cauteries and medicines that are needed.  

Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille  
Here begins the second book on surgical treatments.  

Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;  
We have told you in the first chapter about all the diseases for which fire cautery or burning medicine is needed, as well as the occasions, causes, instruments, and forms of the cauteries.  

et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.  
And I have organized that chapter from head to foot, and I will follow the same approach in this chapter so that what is sought can be found more easily.  

Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.  
And before I begin, it is necessary, dear son, that you understand that there is more danger and fear in this chapter than in the first about cauteries, and therefore it requires greater caution.  

Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;  
For in the operations described in this chapter, there is often blood loss when opening a vein, making an incision on an abscess, treating wounds, extracting arrows, making an incision on a stone, and similar procedures.  

ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.  
Where there is risk and fear, and death comes to many.  

Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.  
And I warn you not to undertake anything foolish.  

Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.  
For many types of people come for treatment.  

si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;  
Some come who are so distressed by their illness that they die easily from the despair they feel about their disease and its severity.  

et de ces doit on avoir paor.  
And of these, one should be afraid.  

Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:  
And among them are those who pretend to be rational and say:  

«atendez, je sui garis»;  
“Wait, I am cured”;  

et li maladie est despitouse.  
but the illness is dire.  

Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;  
You should not consent to those who come to you with such behavior, but place greater value on your honor than on your greed, and act not foolishly but wisely in matters you are certain of, and from which you can gain profit and reputation.  

et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;  
And use prognosis and indication in treating your patients so that healing is achieved.  

et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.  
And this will help you gain good reputation, glory, and a lasting memory of praise.  

Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.  
Dearest son, may Our Lord grant you good understanding and righteousness, and may He inspire you with the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.  

Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.  
Now I have organized this chapter, dividing it into sections, as I did in the chapter on cauteries, arranged from head to foot, so that you may more easily find what you need.  

dou chief plein d’aigue  
On the head filled with water  

Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;  
Know that this condition often occurs in children during childbirth when the delivery compresses the head of the child too strongly.  

et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.  
And sometimes it arises from an unknown cause.  

Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;  
And I have never seen this condition except in children, and in all those I have seen, death came quickly.  

et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.  
And therefore, it seems better to me to leave such cases alone.  

Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;  
And I saw a child whose head was full of water, and the head swelled every day so much that he could not bear it;

et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;  
and the moisture increased so much that he died, and this moisture gathered under the bone upon the membrane, between the brain and the bone;

et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;  
and the operation is such that if the moisture is between the brain and the bone, and the swelling is small, you make a wide incision in the middle of the head;

et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;  
and it should be as long as two fingers, so that the moisture flows;

et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:  
and here is the shape of the spatula:

Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:  
If the moisture has increased more, and the swelling is larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:

Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:  
And if the moisture is under the bone, and you see the signs that the seams of the head are open on each side, and the water spurts out when you press it inward with your hand, and this is not concealed from you:

si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:  
then you must make three incisions in the middle of the head in this manner:

Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.  
And after the incision, extract all the moisture outside.

Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;  
Afterward, compress the incisions with cloths and powders, and apply wine and oil, and leave it thus until the fifth day;

puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.  
then untie it, and treat the wound with tents and ointments, and continue compressing the head evenly, and give the patient dry food with little moisture until the body is strengthened and healed.

Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;  
And another method of incision is that you observe where the swelling is evident, and where the water has accumulated;

car aucune fois est elle devant;  
for sometimes it is in the front;

aucune fois derrier;  
sometimes in the back;

aucune fois en destre;  
sometimes on the right;

et aucune fois en senestre.  
and sometimes on the left.

Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;  
Cut therefore where the swelling appears, and where the water is gathered, and cut it as much as you are able;

et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;  
and be careful not to cut the artery;

et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.  
and let there flow a stream of blood, so that the patient does not die from excessive bleeding or evacuation of moisture.

de reume  
of rheum

Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.  
When someone has a disease called "catarrh" in the eyes or chest, and the disease is chronic, and medical treatment does not help, then the final cure is cauterization along with cutting the two arteries.

Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;  
It is necessary, therefore, when you are about to cut them, that the patient leans back his head;

aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;  
then rub the area with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then the patient presses his neck with a cloth;

puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;  
then observe where the veins pulse, and the locations of each one are behind the ears, and slightly recessed;

puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.  
then mark the places with ink, then cut each one with a sharp spatula from two sides, until the cut reaches the bone, and this should be across the width of the head.

Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.  
And if you wish, place the spatula under the artery and cut above it, cutting as if across two fingers.

Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.  
And when the vein is cut, the blood spurts continuously outward.

Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;  
And if the artery is not visible to the touch, you must measure the distance of three fingers, then mark with ink and cut down to the bone;

et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;  
and the amount of blood that must be let out is six cups, and possibly a little more or less, depending on what the patient can bear and the fullness of the artery;

puis regarde la plaie:  
then examine the wound:

s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.  
if any portion of the membrane remains on the bone, cut it so that hot swellings do not form there, then compress the wound and bind it, and treat it with ointment until it is healed.

de emigrainne  
Of migraine  

Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.  
When chronic migraine occurs, along with acute catarrh, due to the moisture of tears and heat in the temples, old stubborn congestion, and similar conditions, and it has been treated by various medical remedies to no avail, then we extract the arteries of the temples and cauterize them, as we have described.  

Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;  
And the method of extracting them is that the patient pulls back the hair from their temples and focuses on the artery that is visible in the temple, for it is clearly evident by its pulsing, though it is less visible in some men who are excessively cold.  

et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;  
And if it is not visible, let the patient compress their neck with a cloth, then rub the area with a coarse cloth, and sprinkle the spot with hot water until the artery becomes clearly visible.  

puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:  
Then take the spatula of which the shape is as follows:  

puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;  
Then lightly peel the skin until you reach the artery, then pull it upward with pincers and carefully separate it from the tissues beneath it on each side.  

et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.  
And if the artery is thin, twist it at the point of the hook, then cut it in that part to the extent of two heads.  

Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.  
For if it is not completely cut, the blood will not flow entirely out.  

Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;  
And let out between six cups and three cups of blood.  

et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;  
And if the artery is large, you must tie it in two places with a strong double silk thread so that putrefaction does not occur before the healing of the wound and the prevention of blood flow.  

puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;  
Then cut the excess portion between the two ties at that very moment, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with a blade-shaped cautery down to the bone so that the heads are completely cut.  

et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.  
And this is the best procedure, provided the patient has no fever and is of a warm temperament.  

Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:  
For cauterization helps to eliminate the moisture:  

por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.  
Thus, it is of greater help for moisture-related conditions.  

Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;  
Alternatively, for the extraction of arteries, one must fill the area with old cotton and apply well-made tents over it.  

et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;  
And when they are untied, treat with dry medicines that promote flesh growth and with tents until it is healed.  

et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;  
And if blood flows from the artery while you are working on it, quickly stop it by cauterization, or fill the area with vitriol and compress it by hand to staunch the blood.  

et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;  
And if you do not have this at hand, place your finger on the spot until the blood coagulates, and sprinkle the area with cold water until the bleeding stops, and compress it as necessary.  

et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.  
And the best and easiest method of artery extraction is to cauterize the vein with this double-edged cutting cautery, but the blades should be quite thick to retain their heat longer.  

Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.
