For when the instrument is too thin, it retains its heat less.  

Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;  
And there should be a space of one finger's thickness between the two blades, and then when you have marked the two places with ink, you place the heated iron on them until it reaches the bone and cut the vein in two places.  

et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;  
And the cuts should be spaced apart because this cautery does not fully solder the wound.  

et c’est li forme dou cautere:  
And this is the shape of the cautery:  

des larmes  
Tears  

Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;  
When tears from the eyes descend from the veins located on the surface of the head, and no medical cure proves effective, and you see the face of the afflicted redden and feel a trembling sensation in the forehead;  

et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.  
and if the eyes are weak and moist such that the hairs of the eyelids have fallen, the eyelids are inflamed and raw from the burning of the tears, then this treatment is needed.  

Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;  
The ancients called this "contused cure," and the procedure involves shaving the afflicted's forehead, then making three incisions evenly along the length of the forehead.  

et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;  
One incision should be as wide as two fingers in the center of the forehead, descending downward to the nose, and the other two on either side above the eyelids, taking care to avoid cutting the arteries located above the eyelids.  

et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;  
Keep your hand away from the line of the two jaws, and each wound should measure the width of three joined fingers.  

et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:  
Prepare a piece of sponge and several cloths to wipe the blood, then use a sharp spatula on both sides as described:  

des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;  
from the incision near the temple to the second incision;  

et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.  
and scrape all the tissue between the two incisions down to the membrane covering the bone, then repeat this from the middle incision to the other side, and then remove the spatula.  

si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:  
Then insert into the first incision the instrument called a "knife-blade," which is very sharp on one side and smooth, not sharp, on the other, shaped as follows:  

Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.  
Place the sharp side toward the flesh and membrane, and the smooth side toward the bone, and insert it until it reaches the middle incision.  

Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;  
Cut all the vessels descending from the head to the eyes so that the incision is continuous to the exposed membrane, and then do the same in the middle incision to the other side.  

et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;  
Then remove the blood evenly and press the area to stop the flow.  

puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;  
Then place a tent of old cotton in each incision and cover with cloths soaked in wine, oil, and vinegar, ensuring that hot abscesses do not form.  

et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
On the third day, loosen the bandage and administer a large quantity of warm water, then treat the wound with basilicon ointment mixed with rose oil and other remedies for healing wounds until fully healed.  

dou reume des eulz  
Of the flux from the eyes  

Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;  
When someone develops an acute cataract regularly, and you see the eyes weak and small, the vision diminished, and the eyelids burnt;  

et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;  
and the hairs fall out, there is deep, sharp pain in the head, and the patient sneezes;  

adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.  
then understand from these symptoms that this matter and cataract originate from several veins, and the best treatment for it is this.  

Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.  
Instruct the patient to shave their forehead, then make a large incision in the middle of the forehead, and another of about one inch in width.  

Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;  
Start the incision from the left temple to the right temple, cutting down to the bone.  

et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;  
Keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that lead to the jaw.  

et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;  
Once the bone is exposed, wipe away all the blood with a sponge, then separate the two edges of the incision and insert old cotton and linen tents.  

puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;  
Then bandage it with cloths moistened with wine and oil, ensuring that no hot abscesses develop.  

quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.  
When it is removed, you must rub the bone until flesh begins to grow, then treat it with drying agents that help generate flesh.  

En teil maniere:  
In this way:  

pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;  
Take two parts wheat flour and four parts colophony, and make a plaster.  

et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.  
Apply it to these wounds to generate flesh everywhere.  

de l’estoupement des oreilles  
Of the blockage of the ears  

Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:  
Everything that falls into the ears is one of four things:  

ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;  
either grains, an insect, a piece of mineral stone or a similar object such as iron;  

ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;  
or seeds, such as barley, beans, or peas;  

ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.  
or flowing substances such as water and vinegar, or similar materials.  

Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.  
When a stone or another type of object falls into the ear that does not fit or grow there, place the ear in the sunlight.  

Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;  
If you see the stone, drip a small amount of violet oil or sesame oil, then proceed with extraction.  

et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;  
Induce sneezing with spices, block the nostrils when the sneezing begins, and place pieces of cloth or wool around the ear.  

et estent l’oreille au desus.  
Extend the ear upward.  

Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;  
Many times it comes out through this treatment.  

et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:  
If it does not come out, proceed with extraction using fine pincers shaped as follows:  

S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;  
If it comes out with the pincers, it is good.  

se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;  
If not, perform the extraction with a fine hook with a small curve.  

et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;  
If it still does not come out, make a small brass tube and insert its end firmly into the ear opening, sealing the area around the tube with soft wax so no air can enter alongside the tube.  

puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;  
Then pull it out forcefully, as it often comes out as we have said.  

et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;  
If it does not come out this way, take birdlime and place it on an appropriate instrument, wrapping it with a bit of cotton.  

puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.  
Press the birdlime onto the stone or object, then pull it out.  

Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;  
If it does not come out through any of these methods, quickly cut the ear before a hot abscess or spasm develops.  

et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;  
The method of incision is to first bleed the patient from the cephalic vein and draw blood according to their strength, then seat the patient between your hands, turn their ear upward, and make a small incision at the root of the ear in the fatty or dependent area.  

et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;  
Make the incision crescent-shaped until you reach the stone, then remove it to the best of your ability and suck the area quickly with your mouth.  

et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Treat it until it is healed.  

Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;  
If it is a grain inside and it swells, proceed with extraction.  

et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:  
If it cannot come out, use a thin, fine spatula shaped as follows:  

et amenistre incision de celui grain.  
Make an incision in the grain.  

Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;  
Do not do this if you think the grain is moist from the dampness of the ear, until you have divided it into many pieces.  

puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.  
Then extract it with fine pincers and by suction, as we have described, so the extraction is eased.  

En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.  
For water that falls into the ear, the patient should first use sneezing with spices and fill the ear with old cotton.  

Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.  
Lie on the ear itself where the water is.  

s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.  
If it comes out this way, it is good.  

se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;  
If not, take several small stones the length of your finger, thin and light, and heat them slightly in the fire.  

et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;  
The patient places one stone in the ear opening, stands on one foot, and strikes the stone in the ear with another stone.  

et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;  
Continue striking stone against stone until all the water comes out, and it will fully exit this way.  

et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;  
If you wish, take a reed, place one end in the ear, and set the other end on fire until most of the reed is burned.  

puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.  
Repeat this with other reeds until all the water comes out, as we described for the stone.  

En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;  
For extracting an insect, if it is small like a flea or similar, treat it as we described in the earlier section.  

mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;  
If it is large enough to be felt, use pincers for extraction.  

et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.  
This is one of the easiest things to remove from the ear.  

En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:  
For extracting worms growing in the ears, if the treatment described in the earlier section and the discussion on distillations does not help, you must inspect the ear in sunlight:  

s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:  
If you see worms, remove them with fine pincers, and if none are visible, take a tube shaped as follows:  

Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.  
It should be narrow at the bottom and wide at the top.  

Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;  
And place the finest tip into the ear according to the severity of the patient's condition, then suck strongly through the tube.  

fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.  
Do this repeatedly until all the worms come out.  

Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;  
And if they do not obey and come out, wrap the tube with cotton as I described in the stone method.  

et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;  
And if they still do not emerge as we have said, administer distillations proven by the ancients for killing worms, and you will find them in the treatise on distillations.  

et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:  
And distill your oils and medicines into the ear with this instrument, the design of which you see here:  

Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;  
Let it be made of silver or brass, narrow below with a small opening, and open above for distillation.  

et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;  
And to press the distillation inside, use a well-made brass instrument for this purpose, and if you wish, take a razor and neatly wrap its tip with cotton.  

puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;  
Then pour your oil or juice, and whatever medicines you desire, into the tube, and let the tube remain in the ear.  

puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;  
Next, insert the razor with the cotton into the tube, and press gently with your hand until the oil is distilled into the depths of the ear.  

et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;  
Let the patient feel it inside, and let the distillation be slightly warmed over a fire before distilling it into the ear.  

et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.  
Ensure it is not too cold, for the medicine would not be as effective.  

de l’estoupement des oreilles  
On the obstruction of ears  

Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;  
Some children are born without any opening in their ears.  

et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;  
And this same thing happens in men due to the obstruction of a wound or flesh growth within the ear, and this obstruction sometimes extends deep into the ear so that it cannot be seen.  

et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.  
And sometimes it occurs slightly outside the opening, where it is clearly visible.  

Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;  
An obstruction that occurs deep within and cannot be seen is difficult to cure in many cases, while for one that is visible, you should expose the patient's ear to the sunlight.  

et regarde dedens:  
And look inside:  

se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:  
If you see the visible obstruction, work on it with this spatula, the design of which is shown here:  

Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;  
Let it be sharp and cutting at both the front and back, but smooth so as not to harm the ear.  

se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.  
If the obstruction is due to a flesh growth or crust in the ear, hold it with fine pincers and cut it lightly until all the flesh is removed.  

Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.  
If the obstruction is deep within the ear, take a fine, light razor, warm it slightly over a fire, and insert it into the ear canal.  

Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;  
If you detect an obstruction causing the patient discomfort in hearing, pierce lightly and ensure not to damage the nerves of the ear.  

puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.  
Then insert a tent into the ear according to the width of the opening, and moisten it with Egyptian ointment.  

Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;  
Do this for several days until the wound is healed, or take a tent and moisten it with rose water, then sprinkle it with crushed vitriol.  

et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;  
If you see the ear swollen, you must remove the tent and replace it with another tent moistened with cerate made of rose oil and wax, until the swelling subsides.  

puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then treat it until it is healed.  

Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.  
If bleeding occurs, soak a sponge and cloth in cold water, place it on the ear, and use other treatments from the distillation treatise to stop the bleeding.  

de la char des papieres  
On the flesh of the eyelids  

Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;  
These growths that appear on the eyelids, whether moist or dry, should be stretched with tongs and pincers and cut with a spatula at their roots.  

puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.  
Then apply crushed vitriol to the spot.  

Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;  
If blood flows, cauterize it with a fine lenticular cautery, and the cautery is more effective after the incision.  

et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;  
And often they return if any part of their roots remains.  

et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.  
But when they are cauterized by fire, their roots are burned and do not grow back.  

de la gresle  
Of hailstones.  

Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;  
Often in the membranes of the eyes appear things that resemble hailstones in their shape and hardness, and for this reason, this illness is called "hailstone," and it is an accumulation of thick moisture in the upper and lower membrane.  

li ovraiges est telz:  
The procedure is as follows:  

pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;  
First, observe whether the hailstone moves from one place to another, which is an easy thing to ascertain.  

fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.  
Then make a wide incision, peel the membrane slightly on each side, take hold of it with forceps, and cut it.  

se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;  
If you cannot cut it without piercing the membrane slightly, it does not harm the patient.  

et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;  
If the incision is large, close it with sutures and treat it until it is healed.  

et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.  
If it is small, do not force it, as the ointment will quickly restore it and generate tissue.  

Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;  
If the hailstone descends inside the ear towards the upper part, invert the membrane, stretch the hailstone with forceps, cut it, and press on both sides.  

et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;  
If the membrane separates due to the incision, this causes no harm.  

et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.  
Once the hailstone is removed, wash the eye with salted water and treat the area with tissue-regenerating medicine until the patient is healed.  

de la graisse des eulz  
Of fat in the eyes.  

Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;  
Exinach is a fat that forms in the tissues of the upper membranes, occurring more often in children than in others, greatly troubling their eyes, causing cataracts in the mornings, and making them unable to look at sunlight because tears flow rapidly to their eyes.  

et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.  
For this reason, they often lie face down and sleep on their faces, causing the membranes under their eyebrows to become moist, swollen, and covered with the Exinach visible in the eye.  

Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.  
When you press the area with your fingers, you can feel the Exinach between them.  

Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;  
The procedure is that the patient rests their head in your lap.  

et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;  
Then take a linen cloth, prepare a tent in the shape of a circle according to the amount of Exinach present in each part, and place it over the area.  

et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;  
Press with your fingers on both sides so that the Exinach is gathered in the center of the circle.  

puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;  
Then, with a sharp spatula, make an incision in the middle of the moisture, wide but no larger than the cut made in ordinary bloodletting.  

et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;  
Cut deep enough through the skin to reach the Exinach.  

et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.  
In many cases, the Exinach emerges from the incision as a piece of white fat.  

Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;  
Remove it using a piece of cloth wrapped around your fingers, turning your hand to the right and left until it is entirely extracted.  

et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.  
Take care not to widen the incision or push the spatula down to the eye, as this may cause injury.  

Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;  
If the Exinach does not appear at the start of the incision, slightly enlarge it until it becomes visible.  

puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.  
Then extract it as described, moisten cloths with vinegar and water, place them on the area, and secure them with bandages.  

Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.  
Some practitioners crush salt and apply it to destroy any remaining moisture.  

Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then treat it until it is healed.  

Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.  
If a hot abscess forms at the site, treat it with soothing plasters until it heals.  

des poilz des papieres  
Of hairs in the membranes.  

Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;  
When unnatural hairs grow in the membranes and become aged, they harm the eyes, causing various conditions such as excessive tearing, softening of the membranes, and whitening of the cornea, ultimately leading to the destruction of the eyes.  

et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:  
The treatment is done in four ways:  

ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.  
By cautery with fire, by sharp medicine as explained in the chapter on cautery, by incision and suturing, or by scissors, as I will now describe.  

Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;  
You must place the patient’s head in your lap, then turn the membrane of the eye with your left hand.  

s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;  
If it is turned, that is good.  

se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;  
If not, insert a needle with a thread into it.  

et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;  
This should be near the edge of the membrane where the hairs grow, next to those hairs; pull the thread upward along with the membrane and turn it with the razor.  

puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;  
Then make an incision underneath the membrane, below the additional hairs, using the cutting spatula, from the large tear duct to the small one.  

puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.  
Then remove the thread and place a small tent of cotton and cloth beneath the membrane; then mark a hook-shaped figure on the membrane, like the leaf of a myrtle, and ensure that the figure matches the amount of membrane you wish to remove, as designated.  

Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;  
Sometimes it is necessary to cut a large amount of the membrane depending on how much the membrane has softened.  

puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;  
Then, with the spatula, cut along the two lines you have marked, starting from the large tear duct to the small one.  

et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;  
Let one of the incisions be near the natural hairs, about the thickness of a root; then insert the forceps into one of the two corners of the wound and peel it all away.  

puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;  
Next, bring the two edges together with a suture using a needle and a fine wool thread, wipe away the blood, and burn the excess thread above the two eyebrows with something sticky, if you wish to do so.  

et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;  
If not, do not worry about it, then leave the suture and the threads in place for three or four days.  

puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;  
Then treat the wound without further sutures using drying and binding substances, for the membrane will lift and heal itself with the closure of the wound, but sutures are safer (as the ancients said), and this procedure is without danger.  

et si a une autre maniere:  
And there is another method:  

et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:  
It is that you mark the membrane with a figure shaped like a myrtle leaf, as we have described, with three separated hooks in the form shown here:  

puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:  
Then cut away the part that protrudes, equally with small tools, following the shape described here:  

Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;  
If you cannot hold the forceps and the matter is uneven, take a needle with a thread and place it in the middle of the figure.  

et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;  
Place another thread near the large tear duct and a second thread near the small one, then gather the threads evenly between your fingers.  

puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;  
Then lift your hand evenly, raising all the skin where you have marked, as we have described, then bring the two edges of the wound together with sutures and treat it until it is healed.  

et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;  
If an abscess forms at the incision, soothe it with wax plasters and similar soothing ointments.  

et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:  
Sometimes, the hairs on the membrane are inverted.  

si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;  
In such cases, you must use the incision method we have described.  

mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.  
But the suturing in both cases is more precise.  

Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:  
The treatment with scissors is as follows:  

et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;  
You invert the membrane and make an incision within it as I have described, then prepare two scissors with skill and two fine threads as long as the membrane and the width of the spatula.  

et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;  
Cut at the two ends of the two sides where you hold the threads.  

puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;  
Then carefully join the two sides over the protruding part of the eye’s membrane and tighten the two scissors firmly on both sides.  

et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.  
Leave it like this for a few days, and the skin that was compressed will die, blacken, and decay until it falls away on its own.  

S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;  
If it delays, cut it with some scissors, then treat it until it is healed;  

et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;  
and when the wound is closed, the skin will be smooth, and the hair will not grow back;  

et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:  
and this is the shape of the two incisions you will make according to this figure, and to this length and width:  

li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;  
the process is such that you take a fine needle, and thread it with a soft and fine silk thread;  

puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;  
then join the ends and tie them together delicately, and let the length of the thread be one palm long;  

puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;  
then prepare another fine silk thread in the hollow instrument briefly, and tie the ends of the thread;  

puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;  
then the patient places their head in your lap;  

et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;  
and let it be near the sunlight so that the procedure is clearly illuminated, for it is a delicate and fine operation, then insert the needle with the hollow instrument at the root of the attached hair, and pierce through the skin swiftly until you pull it over the natural hair;  

puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;  
then draw the hair up to the hollow instrument, and insert it into the hollow instrument, whether it is one, two, three, or several hairs;  

puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.  
then pull back your hand so that the hairs come out with the hollow instrument through the skin along with the natural hair.  

Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;  
And if the hollow instrument is pulled and the hair does not come out with it, you will pull the hollow instrument underneath with the thread you have prepared, until the hollow instrument emerges from the upper hole and you see it with your eyes;  

adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;  
then you will pull the hollow instrument and the thread, and close the eye and leave it closed for two or three days, until the hair takes root in its place and flesh grows over it;  

et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.  
and if the hair is short, accompany it with a long natural hair, and lift it with that one or leave it until it is extended, and then remove it.  

de la porriture de l’oil  
Of the rotting of the eye  

Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:  
When this illness called "aleacrati" or rotting occurs in the eye, there are two types:  

l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.  
one natural, and the other unnatural.  

Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.  
And it occurs due to the closing of a wound, or cutting, or cauterization, and similar causes.  

Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;  
And the method of treatment is that you cut that closure, separate its edges, and place linen pledgets inside, and bind it until it is healed;  

et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.  
and you must not use drying or constricting substances in its treatment.  

Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;  
For if you do this, the illness will return worse than before;  

mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;  
but treat it with softening agents, such as fenugreek;  

et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.
and moisten it with water or mallow and linseed cooked together, and ointments of diacylon melted in one of the oils, and wrap a pledget in it, and treat it with this.  

Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;  
And the key to your treatment is to ensure that it does not close in the same way as before;  

et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.  
and this procedure that we have described is merely to prevent this illness from returning in the form it was before.  

de la char qui vient en l’oil  
Of the flesh that grows in the eye  

Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.  
This disease, which is beneath, is truly called "axacrati," and is both natural and accidental.  

Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;  
The accident arises from a wound, a split, cauterization, and similar things;  

et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;  
and the way of the operation on it is that you take a needle, in which there is a double thread, and pierce it into the flesh, making it go from the left tear duct to the right, so that the thread comes out in two ends from the flesh;  

puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.  
then stretch the flesh above with the needle, and cut it at a width of one spatula.  

Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;  
And if the shape of the eyelid returns as it should, that is good;  

se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;  
if not, take a razor and place it in the split, turn the eyelid, and make two splits on the side inside the eyelid;  

et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;  
and let the ends of the two splits meet at the two corners of the incision you have made, forming an angle so that when they are joined, the shape resembles the letter called "Greek I";  

puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;  
then remove that flesh, to the extent its sides are sharp underneath, from what follows the eyelid, then join the two separated parts and sew them with a woolen thread;  

puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then treat it with the softening medicines and tents we have mentioned, until it is healed.  

Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;  
And if the disease comes from a split, a stitch, or cauterization, you must make a full split beneath the hairs of the eyelid, as previously described;  

puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;  
then separate between the two edges with a tent, as I have said;  

et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;  
and one must perform the operation according to the form of the disease, for it is very diverse in form, and the wise master prepares with all his skill to restore the shape to its natural form;  

et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.  
and the patient himself, according to what is needed in the work and instruments, in several arrangements.  

dou soudement de la papiere  
Of the adhesion of the eyelid  

Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;  
When this adhesion happens to many men in such a way that the upper eyelid is stuck to the white of the eye and cannot move or perform its natural functions, you must then insert the tip of a razor beneath the eyelid and lift it up;  

et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;  
and stretch it with forceps until you cut what is attached with a subtle spatula, which should not be too sharp or too cutting, so that the patient does not suffer or the overly sharp spatula does not harm the eye;  

et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;  
and let your incision, with which you separate that adhesion, be light, so that the eyelid returns to its natural form;  

et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;  
and all that adhesion is healed, and sometimes they use salty water on the eye, then wash it with fresh water and collyrium;  

puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;  
then place a linen tent between the eyelid and the eye, and put on the eye wool soaked in egg white;  

et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and after the third day, use collyrium and soothing remedies until it is healed.  

de l’ungle de l’oil  
Of the nail of the eye  

Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:  
Know that the nail appears in two forms:  

elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;  
it is either fibrous and resembles a hard membrane or another that is not fibrous but appears like frozen white moisture, which cannot be grasped with forceps when touched with iron.  

et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.  
Both types start near the large tear duct and grow little by little until they cover the entire sight, light, and movement of the eye.  

Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;  
And the method of incision is that the patient places his head on your chest, then opens his eyes;  

et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;  
and lift the eyelid with your hand, then grasp the nail with small, curved forceps and pull it upward;  

puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;  
then take a needle and thread it with a horsehair, cowhair, or oxhair, and a strong thread;  

et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;  
and slightly bend the tip of the needle, pierce it through the middle of the nail, passing it through entirely, tie the nail with a thread, stretch it upwards, and scrape the edge of the nail that follows the pupil with the thread, all the way to its root; then cut the remaining part at the tear duct root with a fine spatula and small forceps, leaving the natural flesh of the tear duct untouched so that tears may flow as usual.  

et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;  
And sometimes the nail is removed with just the hook and thread, as we have described;  

puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:  
then it is scraped entirely with the gentle spatula, whose shape is as follows:  

Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;  
And ensure that the spatula does not touch or tear the fleshy membrane, and that the pupil is not pierced.  

et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;  
After the incision, sprinkle a little crushed salt into the eye and apply collyrium made from litharge, and leave it until the next day.  

puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then treat it with what is necessary until it is healed.  

Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;  
And if the nail is not fibrous, and you cannot insert the needle or use the hook, this type of nail is often treated with medicines.  

et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:  
These grow as I have explained earlier, and if you wish to cut it, open the patient's eye and use a light, slightly sharp spatula as follows:  

Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;  
And subtly lift the nail upward, and if you see it thinning and the removal seems close, drop collyrium made from litharge, red collyrium, and crushed salt into the eye from your mouth, and cover the eye until the next day.  

puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.  
Then resume the work according to the same procedure until it is completely removed.  

Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
If anything interferes in the eye, such as a hot abscess, then leave it and first treat the hot abscess until it is healed, then resume the work as before until it is healed.  

Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;  
If the appearance of flesh from the tear duct greatly disturbs the eye, suspend it with a hook, cut part of it but not all, so that tears may still flow.  

puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.  
Then drop into the eye red collyrium made from litharge.  

de la char qui naist sus la prunelle  
Of the flesh that grows over the pupil  

Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;  
In the eyes of some men, red flesh sometimes grows, covering the pupil, constricting the eyelids, turning them outward, and resembling a pomegranate flower.  

et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;  
And the procedure is for the patient to rest his head on your chest, then open his eyes, and grasp all that flesh with suitable hooks, holding it firmly;  

puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;  
then cut the foremost flesh, continuing to cut with a razor until the end, being careful not to injure the eye during the procedure;  

et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;  
and let the incision be made with the spatula as we have described for the nail, and with small forceps, with which the debris is removed, as the shape described after this chapter demonstrates.  

et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;  
And when the incision is complete and all the flesh is removed, fill the eye with crushed salt or drop in red collyrium and similar corrosive medicines, and place cotton soaked in egg white over the eye to protect it from hot abscesses.  

et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;  
If anything remains, and hot blood rises, and you fear a hot abscess, leave the eye and treat the abscess with soothing remedies for hot abscesses.  

puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.  
Then return to your work until it is healed, and proceed similarly whenever flesh accumulates in the eye in this manner.  

Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;  
But nevertheless it is necessary that you alleviate the treatment of each weak eye by the natural method;  

et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;  
and by the accidental method, through the use of iron instruments;  

et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.  
and do not place your hand on any of these operations until you see that this member can endure the procedure.  

des voines des eulz  
Of the veins of the eyes  

Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.  
Sebel are red veins that are spread over the eye, and they obstruct vision and weaken the eye permanently.  

Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;  
It is necessary first that you observe whether the eye, in which sebel is present, is strong, and that there is no other disease except for the sebel;  

adonques le coil en teil maniere:  
then treat it in this manner:  

comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:  
command the patient to place their head against your breast, then tie off those veins with a thread according to your skill, and let the thread be fine and doubled in this way:  

Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:  
And let there be two threads arranged step by step on one body in this way:  

puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;  
then as you treat them, cut those veins subtly, and wipe the blood little by little, until you see those veins moving away from the eye;  

et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;  
and ensure that you do not injure the eye with the tips of the spatulas, and perform this procedure at midday before the sun, and be very precise in your work so that you cut nothing except those veins;  

et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.  
and when you have done this, instill green and red collyrium into the eye to destroy what remains of the sebel.  

Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;  
And if you are unable to complete all of this at that time, then apply a poultice to the eye made of things that soothe the pain of the eyes, and leave it for some days until the pain subsides and there is assurance of no hot abscess, then resume in the way described earlier until it is healed;  

et c’est li forme des forces:  
and this is the form of the procedures:  

de la fistule de l’oil  
Of the fistula of the eye  

Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:  
The doctors call this fistula "arissati":  

quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.  
when you treat it with cautery and sharp burning medicine as I have described above, and it is not healed, then it is necessary to incise the abscess where it should be opened and draw out all the moisture that is there, until the bone is exposed.  

Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;  
And when the bone is exposed, and you see the corruption and the blackness, then scrape it with the instrument of which this is the form;  

et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:  
and it is called the "rough head," and let it be made of Indian steel with a rounded head, and let it be pointed like a file as it is in this form:  

Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;  
And place it on the area of the corrupted bone, then turn it between your fingers, and press your hand a little until you know that the corruption has been removed;  

et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.  
and do this several times, then restore the area with drying medicines.  

se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;  
if the area is closed, and flesh grows there, and the body of the opening is sealed, and it remains so for forty days, and it does not reopen and does not form an abscess, and no bad conditions occur, know that it is healed;  

se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:  
if not, then there is no other recourse than to bring the fistula back to the opening of the nostril in this way:  

et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:  
and this is to expose the bone a second time with iron and sharp medicines, and when it is exposed, take a drill in this form, and let its head be made of iron with three angles, and let its shaft be tapered to the end as you see here:  

puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;  
then place it on the bone near the lacrimal duct, and move your hand a little away from the eye, then turn the drill until it pierces the bone and the patient feels it by the air escaping if they place their hand over their nostril;  

et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;  
and then restore the area with drying medicines as I have taught you, and when the flesh grows and the area hardens, the matter will go to the nostril;  

si est plus legiere chose au malaide.  
and this is a much easier condition for the patient.  

de l’issue de l’oil  
Of the discharge from the eye  

Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;  
When the eye opens outward entirely and there is no obstruction to the nostril or shrinkage, it is necessary that you bind the patient;  

puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;  
then treat it, then apply cupping glasses to the nape without incision to draw out, then place on the eye a poultice made of acacia, aloe, incense, and sarcocol, and then bind the eye and apply the poultice with bandages and cloths;  

et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;  
and the method of the cloths is that you take sufficiently soft cloths, fold each one in four, and then place them one on top of another according to the quantity needed for the eye;  

puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;  
then bind it tightly over with a firm bandage, and repeat the cupping to draw without incision;  

puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;  
then remove the cupping glasses and leave the eye bound day and night, and if the binding becomes loose, it is necessary to tighten it further;  

puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;  
then remove the binding after the day and night, and if you see the eye recovering, it is good;  

se ce non;  
if not;  

si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then repeat the poultice, cloths, binding, and cupping until it is healed.  

dou derrompement de toile uvee  
Of the rupture of the uveal membrane  

Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;  
When a rupture occurs in the uveal membrane, it opens, and a swelling appears like a grain of resin, and it is frightful to behold;  

adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;  
then if you wish to cut it, the procedure is such that you insert a needle at the root of the lower part up to the upper one, then insert another needle with a doubled thread near the lacrimal area;  

et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;  
and pierce it there, and leave the first needle in place according to the arrangement;  

puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;  
then cut the area of the double thread and tie part of the uveal membrane around it, and bind it tightly, then remove the needle and place on the eye wool soaked in egg white;  

et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;  
and leave it until the thread falls off with the uveal membrane, then treat the eye with comforting remedies until the wound is healed;  

et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.  
and sometimes the wound is restrained by the uveal membrane on each side with a ring of cloth, until it is healed.  

Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;  
And if the eye swells significantly, pierce it with a fine spatula that reaches deep into the eye, and drain the albugineous moisture so that the eye settles and reenters immediately;  

puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then bind it until it is healed.  

de la bowe de l’oil  
Of the clouding of the eye  

Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;  
This disease, which is called "alcunnati," is nothing but clouding that gathers in the eye, resembling descending water, but it is not water;  

et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;  
and the method for examining it is to have the patient sit on a prepared and upright seat, then take their head between your two hands, and move it until you see the clouding rise to the surface in your view;  

puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;  
then ensure it remains visible, and does not descend, and the light becomes unobstructed, and the patient sees things as they used to;  

et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.  
and if it does not descend below, know that it is water, and if the descent of the clouding is not arranged as we have said.  

si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;  
then make the patient sit between your hands, then take a fine spatula and cut slightly into the corneal membrane along the continuation of the conjunctiva with the corneal membrane and the corona, until the clouding emerges;  

et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.  
and when it has emerged, instill into the eye warm water mixed with honey, or water in which fenugreek has been boiled with honey, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.  

des aigues de l’oil  
Of the waters of the eye  

Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;  
We have already the descriptions of the waters in their division, and what is necessary to pierce them;  

si en oevre selonc la santeit.  
thus it is done according to health.  

Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;  
You must seat the patient between your crossed hands, away from the light of the sun, and bind the healthy eye tightly;  

puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;  
then place the eyelid of the eye in your left hand if the eye is the left one, or in your right hand if the eye is the right one;  

puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;  
then take in your right hand, if the eye is the left one, the instrument called "almagda," or in your left hand, if the eye is the right one;  

puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;  
then place the point of the instrument beside the crown by the width of a hair in the whiteness of the eye at the part of the lesser tear duct, then press the instrument called "almagda" skillfully, and turn your hand until it pierces the whiteness of the eye, and feel that the almagda reaches the empty space;  

et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;  
and it is necessary that the depth of the almagda's path be the same as the space from the pupil to the end of the blackness;  

et c’est li corone de l’oil;  
and this is the crown of the eye;  

si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.  
thus you will see the membrane in that place due to the clarity of the corneal layer, and you can insert the instrument to where the water is, then expel it one pathway after another.  

se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.  
If the water descends immediately, the patient sees before themself and the instrument in their eye.  

Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;  
Then let them rest a little, and if the water rises again, apply force with the instrument, and when it is fixed inside and does not rise, withdraw the almagda lightly while turning your hand little by little;  

et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.  
and then place a bit of powdered gem salt in the water, and rinse the eye with it inside.  

Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.  
Then place outside the eye cotton or wool soaked in rose oil and egg white, and bind it with the healthy eye.  

Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.  
We, and those of our time, apply crushed cumin with egg white.  

Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:  
And if the almagda cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, for there are some people whose eyes are too hard, you must take the instrument called "alberit," whose shape is as follows:  

Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;  
And pierce only the conjunctiva, and do not go too deep, but make a subtle opening, then insert the almagda, as we have said;  

et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;  
and at the completion of the procedure, prepare a suitable bed for the patient, where they may sleep on their back in a dark place;  

et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;  
and let them be deprived of all movements, take light food, and not move their head either to the right or the left, and let them be bound according to their condition until the third day;  

puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;  
then unbind them in the same dark house, test their vision, and make them see some objects, and then reapply the binding until the seventh day;  

et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.  
and it is not necessary for you to do this during the treatment or immediately after the incision, but you must alleviate it, for the water rises quickly.  

se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;  
If hot abscesses appear, unbind the eye before the seventh day, and treat it with something that soothes abscesses;  

et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.  
and when it is calmed, unbind the vision and place a small cloth on the face to cover it from light, and let them remain in that dark house.  

Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;  
And then leave the house little by little, and return to their usual activities;  

et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.  
and know that no disciples should meddle in this matter.  

Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;  
And one came to us from Iraq, who told us that in their country they performed a pierced almagda, through which the water is drawn out, but I never saw such a thing in our land, nor did I ever read it in the books of the ancients;  

et par aventure c’est une novele chose.  
and perhaps it is a new invention.  

Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;  
And these are the likenesses of the forms of the almagda, so that those who do not know them may see them;  

et soient d’arain proprement:  
and let them be made properly of bronze:  

Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.  
And let their heads have the same subtlety, and their ends be in three sharp angles.  

de la char sor le neis  
Of the flesh upon the nose  

Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;  
Sometimes various types of flesh grow on the nose, some of which resemble scorpions with many legs;  

et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.  
and there are those where the flesh is ulcerated with a reddish color, and others with soft flesh of good color.  

En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;  
In the case of soft flesh that is not ulcerated, you must seat the patient between your hands facing the sun;  

et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;  
and open their nostrils, apply the salve to the flesh, and extract it;  

pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.  
then cut away what you can safely handle with a subtle, sharp spatumile, until you are sure that all the flesh is removed.  

Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;  
And if anything remains that cannot be cut, gently open it with a delicate instrument, so that nothing is left.  

et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;  
And if excessive bleeding or a hot abscess occurs, treat it as necessary;  

et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.  
And if it is a malignant abscess, act quickly and cauterize it until the bleeding is stopped and all the flesh is removed, then pour vinegar and water or wine into the nose.  

Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;  
If the nose opens, and moisture flows down to the palate, know that it is healed;  

et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:  
and if moisture does not flow as it should, know that flesh has grown on the underlying bone, which the instrument cannot reach to cut.  

adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;  
Then you must insert a slightly thick linen thread, knotted at short intervals, with each knot spaced about a finger's width or less.  

et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;  
The patient must place the end of the thread in their nostril as best as they can and pull it while inhaling until it comes through the nose into the mouth.  

et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;  
This is often done by schoolchildren, and it is an easy thing for anyone willing to do it.  

puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.  
Then hold the end coming out of the nose in one hand and the other end from the mouth in the other hand, and rub them alternately over the knots in the thread.  

Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;  
Do this until you know the knots have broken down the flesh, then pull out the thread, wipe away the blood, moisten the thread with Egyptian ointment, and reinsert it into the nose as before.  

fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;  
Do this for three days or more until the ointment corrodes all the remaining flesh.  

et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;  
Then place a lead tube in the nose for some days until it is healed, and if drying medicines are needed, use them.
