et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:  
This is the shape of the instrument used to purge the head, through which oils and medicines are distilled into the nose:  

Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;  
It should be made of silver or bronze, resembling an open lamp, shaped like a tube, with similar conduits.  

et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;  
And if you wish, make a closed tube, and let the instrument be ready for purging the head.  

et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.  
It should have a handle at the top to hold it while heating the oil or other liquid.  

de la char sor le neis  
Of the flesh on the nose  

Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;  
Sometimes a condition called "telul" appears at the tip of the nose, growing larger over time until it becomes visible and unsightly.  

et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;  
Therefore, you must cut it at the beginning and remove it completely, then apply a cautery or a burning medicine to the area.  

et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:  
And if cutting is delayed until it becomes large, check whether it is hard, reddish in color, and poorly textured:  

si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;  
If so, do not touch it with iron, for it is an ulcerated abscess, and cutting it sometimes brings great harm to the patient.  

et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.  
But if the abscess is soft to the touch, not reddish in color, and you see that it can be entirely cut, empty the patient and cut it without fear, then treat the area with drying and astringent substances.  

quant li neis est copez et cosus  
When the nose is cut and sewn.  

Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.  
Know that when a discontinuity occurs in one of these complex cartilages, it rarely heals, except in some people.  

Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;  
Thus, when this happens to someone, you must check if the wound is fresh with all its blood.  

et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;  
Then join the two edges with a suture and treat it until it heals.  

et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;  
And if the edges are already separated on both sides, you must scrape all parts of their surface until they bleed, then join the two edges with a suture, tighten it, and sprinkle it with powdered dragon's blood and ground incense.  

et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Place over the powders a piece of strong plaster or another adhesive plaster, and leave it until it falls off by itself, then treat it with ointment until it heals.  

Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:  
The method of suturing is that you join the discontinuity:  

ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;  
Either with needles, as we described for abdominal sutures;  

ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.  
Or with thread, as I have explained to you.  

des apostemes des levres  
On abscesses of the lips.  

A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;  
Many people develop hard abscesses inside the lips, resembling vetch seeds, sometimes smaller, sometimes larger.  

adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;  
Then you must turn the lips, incise each node, grab it with forceps, and cut it into pieces.  

puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;  
Then fill the site of the incision with powdered vitriol until the bleeding stops.  

et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then wash it with vinegar and treat the area with drying agents until it heals.  

de la char des gencives  
On the flesh of the gums.  

Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;  
Often, flesh grows on the gums, which the ancients called "albulus."  

si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;  
You must hold it with forceps, cut it at its root, and let the pus or blood flow.  

puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;  
Then apply powdered vitriol or other astringent and drying powders to the site.  

et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:  
And if that flesh grows back after the incision, as often happens, cut it again and cauterize it.  

si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;  
It does not grow back after cauterization.  

et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.  
These are the forms of instruments for cutting.  

des sordens  
On tartar.  

Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;  
Sometimes, ugly and rough crusts accumulate on the crowns of the teeth, inside the mouth, between the gums.  

et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;  
Sometimes the teeth are black, yellowish, or green, to the point where the decay spreads to the gums, and the teeth become foul-smelling.  

si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;  
You must seat the patient between your hands, with his head in your lap, and scrape the teeth until the crusts are entirely removed.  

et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;  
Do the same with the blackness, the greenness, the yellowness, and other stains, until they are cleaned.  

et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;  
If you remove it all at the first scraping, it is good.  

se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;  
If not, start again on the second and third days, until you have completely scraped it away.  

et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;  
Know that teeth require various forms of instruments for scraping, depending on what the work demands, because scrapers for the outer surfaces of teeth have different shapes from those used between the teeth.  

et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.  
Have these and other forms ready with you.  

Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;  
When treating a tooth for pain, you must delay extraction as long as possible, because it should not be done hastily.  

car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.  
For it is a very precious substance, and until then there is no justification for scraping.  

Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.  
So when the patient is forced to extract a tooth, you must be certain of which tooth is causing the pain.  

Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;  
Often, the pain deceives the patient, who thinks it is in a healthy tooth and has a good tooth extracted.  

et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;  
Yet the pain does not cease until the diseased one is removed, for we have often seen this with noblemen.  

et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;  
When you are certain of the painful tooth, you must scrape around the tooth with a sharp spatula to protect the gum on all sides.  

puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;  
Then move it with your fingers or fine forceps, little by little, until it is well loosened, then firmly secure the forceps.  

et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.  
Let the patient’s head rest in your lap between your knees, and hold him steady so that he does not move.  

Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.  
Afterward, extract the tooth straight without breaking it, and if it does not come out at first, take one of these instruments, insert it gently on each side, and move it as you did before.  

Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;  
And if the tooth is pierced and decayed, you must fill it with cloth where the holes are.  

et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;  
And tighten it gently with forceps so that it does not break under the pressure.  

et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.  
You must work very carefully around the gum to loosen the tooth.  

Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.  
Take care not to break it, leaving a piece behind, which could cause the patient even greater pain than before because of the malice of the root.  

Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;  
Beware not to act like ignorant practitioners, who through haste and recklessness sometimes break the tooth, failing to apply what we have described.  

mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;  
Instead, they sometimes cause great illness due to roots left behind or the broken tooth, as we have often seen.  

et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;  
When the tooth is extracted, wash the site with wine, vinegar, and salt.  

et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;  
If there is bleeding, as often happens, fill the site with powdered vitriol.  

et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.  
And if that does not work, cauterize it.  

Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;  
The forms of the instruments used to loosen the teeth first must have long points and thick handles so that they do not bend when extracting the tooth.  

et ce sont les formes:  
And these are their forms:  

Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.  
They must be robust so that they do not bend during extraction, made of well-crafted steel, and toothed to hold firmly.  

de la racine des dens  
On the roots of teeth.  

Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;  
When the root remains after extraction, you must place cotton soaked in butter on the site for one or two days until it softens, then use the forceps called "algefri," whose head resembles a bird's beak.  

et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:  
They should have an interior made like a file, and this is their form:  

Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:  
If the roots do not come out with these forceps, you must uncover the flesh entirely around the root and use the instrument called "althali," which is a lever, and this is its form:  

Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;  
It must be strong and thick so that it does not break, and if the root comes out with it, that is good.  

se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:  
If not, use all the instruments, whose forms are shown hereafter:  

Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:  
And use this instrument, which has two prongs, whose form is as follows:  

et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:  
And other tools used earlier for the treatment of teeth, and this instrument resembling large forceps, whose form is as follows:  

Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;  
This instrument must be strong so that it does not break, and know that there are many tools for teeth.  

et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;  
Likewise, there are other tools not listed here.  

et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:  
A wise and skilled master devises his own tools according to what his work and the diseases show him, for there are conditions for which the ancients did not specify instruments due to their diversity. If part of the tooth or other bones breaks or rots, search for the appropriate instruments, as I have told you, and use gestures, whose form is as follows:  

Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;  
They must be robust and firm to hold the bone so that it does not slip but can be held and removed.  

et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:  
Then restore the site with appropriate medicines, and if there is a small amount of rot in the bone, scrape it with this instrument.  

Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:  
When a tooth appears out of alignment with the natural body, and its form is unsightly, especially in young women, you must determine whether the tooth has grown after the others and is not in the correct position and cannot be filed or ground down.  

adonques lou raie;  
Then it must be removed.  

et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:  
And if it is loose alongside the tooth, take this instrument, whose form is as follows, resembling a small beak and made of sharp steel at the tip.  

Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:  
And cut it little by little over several days because of the hardness of the tooth, and so that you do not move the others; and if it is apparent that it can be filed, file it with a file shaped like this:  

et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;  
and it is like the file used to make needles;  

et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;  
and file the tooth little by little over several days gently, so that it does not move until it falls;  

puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.  
then smooth it in the end with a rasp, and if the tooth is too sharp and injures the tongue, it is necessary to file its roughness until it is even, so that it neither injures the tongue nor disrupts speech.  

quant li dent lochent  
when the teeth are loose  

Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;  
When the front teeth are loose, either from a blow or a fall, and the patient cannot bite down on what they eat without them falling, and you have treated them with astringent medicines, and that is not enough;  

si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;  
then it is necessary to restrain them with a gold wire, for silver wire turns green and rots, but gold does not change at all;  

et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;  
and let the wire be moderate, neither too thick nor too thin, according to the size of the space between the teeth;  

et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;  
and if you want to align the teeth, take the wire and insert it doubled between the two healthy teeth, then place the ends between the loose teeth, if there is one or several, until you carefully reach the healthy tooth on the other side;  

puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;  
then begin again the wrapping up to the part where you started, and tighten your hand subtly and carefully, so that it does not move at all;  

et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.  
and let your binding be at the root of the tooth so that it cannot come loose.  

Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;  
Then cut the ends of the wire with pincers, assemble them, and push them between the healthy teeth, placing them so that they do not injure the tongue;  

et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;  
and then leave it tightened like this as long as it can hold, and if it loosens or the wire breaks, tighten it again with another wire;  

si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:  
so it will remain and serve like this for all its time, and this is the form of the teeth and the arrangement of the two healthy teeth and the two loose ones, as you see:  

Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;  
And when the tooth falls, put it back in its place, as fresh as possible, just as we have said;  

et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.  
and let no one intervene who is not wise and patient, and sometimes one makes the shape of a tooth from cow bone, places it where the missing one was, and binds it as we have said, and it stays and serves for a long time like this.  

de coper lou liien de la lengue  
Of cutting the tie of the tongue  

Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;  
Sometimes there is this tie beneath the tongue that is natural, and one is born like this;  

ou par accident de plaie soudee;  
or from the accident of a wound that has fused;  

et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;  
and the operation is such that you open the patient’s mouth, place their head in your lap, and lift their tongue;  

puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;  
then cut the fibrous tie broadly, so that the tongue is freed from its attachment, and if there is hardness or a knot, and it is from a fused wound, use a hook and cut broadly at that attachment;  

et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;  
and be careful that the incision is not too deep, because of the artery underneath;  

et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;  
and when you have finished, wash the area with rose water and vinegar, or cold water, then place under the tongue a linen tent;  

et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.  
and let the patient keep it there every night, so that the area does not fuse.  

Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;  
And if a flow of blood occurs, place powdered vitriol on the area;  

et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;  
and if the blood overwhelms you, cauterize it with a speckled cautery iron, which is good for this;  

puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,  
then treat it with other remedies until it is healed,  

et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;  
and if you see it as reddish, black, or hard, and the patient does not feel it, do not touch it, for it is a chancre;  

et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;  
and if it tends toward whiteness, and there is moisture, apply a hook to it, open it with a fine spatula, and free it on both sides;  

et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;  
and if blood overwhelms you during the procedure, place powdered vitriol on it until it is staunched, then return to your work until you have removed all the pus;  

puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then wash the area with vinegar and brine, and treat it with other remedies until it is healed.  

des apostemes de la gorge  
Of the abscesses of the throat  

Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:  
Sometimes lumps appear in the throat, called "godath," properly referred to as the two tonsils, and when you treat them as we described in the section on cutting, and they do not heal, take heed:  

se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.  
if it is a hard abscess of little size and reddish color, do not touch it with iron.  

Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;  
And if it is red and the root is swollen, do not touch it with iron, also because of the risk of bleeding;  

mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;  
but leave it until it matures, and then you will open it, or it will rupture on its own.  

et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.  
And if it is of white rounded color and the root is delicate, prepare the instrument for cutting, but first ensure that the hot abscess is resting and calmed.  

Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;  
Then have the patient sit in front of the sun, their head in your lap, open their mouth, have the assistant hold them with their hands, and press down the tongue with the instrument, shaped as follows:  

et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:  
and let it be of fine silver or bronze, shaped like a knife:  

Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;  
When you press the tongue with this instrument and see the abscess, take a hook and insert it into the tonsil, and pull it upward as much as you can;  

et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;  
and pull some tissue with it, then cut it with the instrument shaped like this, resembling forceps;  

et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:  
and both ends are curved, one facing the other, very sharp, and made of Indian or Andalusian steel:  

Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:  
And if you do not have this instrument available, cut it with pincers, shaped as follows:  

Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;  
And let it be sharp on one side, and not on the other;  

et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;
and when you have cut one tonsil, cut the other in the same manner, and after the incision, have the patient gargle with warm water, and water with vinegar, and if bleeding occurs, have the patient gargle water, or boiled pomegranate rinds, or myrtle leaves, and similar substances, until the bleeding stops;  

puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;  
then treat it until it heals;  

et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.  
and sometimes other abscesses form in the throat beyond the two tonsils, then cut them just as you would the two tonsils.  

Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;  
And I treated a woman for an abscess that had formed in her throat, namely a small abscess;  

et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.  
and it had nearly closed her entire throat, so that the woman could not breathe because her airway was blocked, and she could neither eat nor drink, and she would have died if she had remained like this for one or two days.  

Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.  
And the abscess had swollen so much that it had forced out two branches through the two openings of her nose.  

Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;  
I hastened immediately, inserted a hook into one nostril, then pulled it out, and extracted a large amount of pus;  

puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;  
then I did the same in the other nostril, opened her mouth, and pressed down her tongue;  

aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;  
afterward, I inserted the hook into the abscesses and cut a part of them, and only a little blood came out;  

et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;  
and thus the woman’s airway was unblocked, and she began immediately to drink water and then wine, and I did not stop cutting at that abscess over a long time;  

et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;  
and the abscess kept regrowing and refilling the space I had emptied, until it became very large again;  

adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:  
then I pierced it and cauterized it inside the throat:  

ensi demora sens croistre;  
thus it remained without growing;  

et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.  
and I left that region, and I do not know what God did for her after me.  

de l’uve  
Of the uvula  

Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;  
When rheum descends to the uvula, and it is swollen and elongated, it is called "perpendicular";  

et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».  
and if it is swollen and round below, it is called "uvula."  

Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;  
When it has been treated as we described in the section on cutting, and the treatment does not help, and you see that the hot abscess has calmed and it is delicate, then it is necessary to cut it;  

et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;  
and this one, which is round, compact, and not elongated;  

et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.  
and if it is red, reddish, or black, you must avoid cutting it.  

Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.  
For there is great danger to the patient.  

Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;  
It is necessary, therefore, when you see it, according to the manner I have described, concerning its whiteness and length, to seat the patient facing the sun and press his tongue with the instrument we mentioned earlier;  

puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.  
then insert the hook into the uvula, draw it down, and cut it with one of the two instruments I mentioned in the incision of the tonsils.  

Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;  
And it is necessary that you cut nothing but the excess that goes beyond the natural limit;  

car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;  
for if you cut more, it will harm the voice and speech;  

et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.  
and after the incision, use what we have described in the incision of the tonsils and treat it until it is healed.  

Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.  
And if the patient fears the cutting, then you must use a device for cauterization to alleviate their fear.  

Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.  
And the method of cauterization is very precise.  

Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;  
And the patient must rest his head on your chest, then you press his tongue with the instrument we mentioned in the chapter on cauterization, and prepare it with hot quicksilver water, ensuring it is neither too thick nor too clear;  

et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:  
and fill the tip of this instrument, which is of the following form:  

Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;  
And at the tip there is a cavity where the medicine is placed, similar to the tip of a spoon, and place the instrument with the medicine upon the uvula;  

et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;  
and the patient should lie on his side so that saliva and mucus flow from his mouth along with the medicine, preventing it from descending into the throat and causing harm;  

puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;  
then hold your hand with the medicine and press it upon the uvula for half an hour until you see it blackened and the stinging of the medicine has subsided;  

et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;  
and if you wish, take cotton, wrap it around an instrument, soak the cotton in the medicine, and place the instrument with the cotton above the uvula so that the cotton adheres to it;  

et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.  
and do this often until the cauterization is complete, then let it dry, and it will fall off after four or five days.  

Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;  
And if it is necessary to restart the cauterization with the medicine, then restart it, and after the cauterization, wipe around the uvula with cotton dipped in butter, and clean what surrounds the medicine;  

et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and it should be moistened with cold water and treated with gargles until it is healed.  

Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;  
This treatment is safer than incision and cauterization;  

s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;  
if it is treated with fumigation in this manner, take calamint, hyssop, oregano, rue, chamomile, oats, and similar herbs, and gather them all or some of them in a pot, add garlic, and bring to a boil;  

et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:  
and the pot should be well sealed and made of strong clay, and in the middle of the pot there should be an instrument head shaped in this manner:  

Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;  
And it should be made of silver or brass, and one of its ends should be placed in the patient’s mouth so that the vapor rises to the uvula through the tube, until the uvula is desensitized;  

aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;  
then repeat this often until the uvula dries, and ensure that you do not perform this at the beginning of the arrival of a hot abscess, as many complications may arise;  

et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.  
and this should only be done during the decline of the hot abscess.  

Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;  
And if this instrument is not available, take a tube and insert into its tip an eggshell so that the patient’s mouth does not become too hot;  

car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.  
for the eggshell prevents the vapor from harming the mouth, and this is a good and safe treatment.  

Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;  
Many times, a bone or fish spine, or some other object, gets stuck in the throat;  

si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;  
so you must extract what you can see, pressing the tongue in the sunlight with the instrument, so that you can locate the object;  

et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;  
and for what you cannot see and is lodged in the throat, you must make the patient vomit before the food is digested in the stomach;  

par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;  
perhaps the lodged object will emerge through vomiting;  

ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;  
or the patient should swallow a piece of sponge, a piece of navelwort, a lettuce root, or a morsel of dry bread;  

et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;  
and tie a thread to the sponge and have them swallow it;  

et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;  
and when it reaches the spot, it will adhere, and then you will pull it out;  

et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:  
and if it does not come out with what we have described, then take a lead instrument shaped as follows:  

Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;  
And let the instrument be curved at the tip so that it can enter the throat more easily, and let the tip be elevated;  

et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;  
and ensure that you do not touch the epiglottis to avoid causing coughing, and do not push the bone further inward;  

et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;  
and better yet, let the patient himself guide the instrument, so that he can target where the object is lodged;  

si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.  
then push it down, or pull it out evenly with the instrument, until it is removed.  

De la sansue de la gorge  
Concerning the leech in the throat  

Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;  
Sometimes the leech is treated, as I have said in the division, through medicinal cures;  

et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.  
and when this does not work, then inspect the throat of the patient in the sunlight, after pressing his tongue with the instrument I have described to you.  

Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.  
And if you see the leech, remove it with a small hook or with fine pincers suitable for this purpose.  

Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.  
And if this does not work, take a hollow tube and insert it into the patient’s throat, then place a hot iron at the end of the tube, and do this repeatedly.  

Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.  
And have the patient avoid drinking water all day.  

Puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;  
Then take a full glass of cold water, open his mouth, pour it in without swallowing, and move it around with his hand often;  

et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.  
and as soon as the leech senses the water, it will fall off.  

Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;  
And if it does not fall off as we have described, fumigate the patient with asafoetida using the instrument I described for fumigating the uvula;  

fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.  
Do this many times, as the leech will soon fall.  

Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;  
And the method of fumigation is to take a pot containing live coals, cover the pot with a lid pierced in the middle, and in this hole place the end of the instrument;  

puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;  
then add the fumigation, and the patient places the end of the tube in his mouth, closing his mouth so that the smoke does not escape but instead reaches the leech;  

et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;  
and the leech will fall immediately, and if it does not, repeat the fumigation many times;  

et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;  
and have the patient endure thirst, eat salty and pungent things, and refrain from drinking water;  

et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.  
and then it will be necessary for the leech to be expelled by this procedure.  

Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;  
And the shape of the instrument used to extract the leech, when it can be seen, is like curved pincers designed to enter the throat;  

et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;  
and it resembles the beak of a swan, with a rough texture like a file, so that whatever it grips, it cannot let go;  

et vez ci la forme:  
and here is the shape:  

Li chapistres des apostemes  
The chapters on abscesses  

Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;  
There are many types of abscesses, as described later in this book, differing in perforation and cutting;  

et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.  
and these fall into two categories: one that retains its form and moisture.  

Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.  
And the second type depends on the location they occupy in the body.  

Car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.  
For an abscess in the head differs from one in the fundament, and an abscess in fleshy areas differs from one near joints, and each requires its specific treatment.  

Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;  
And there are abscesses that should not be pierced until the pus is mature according to its completion;  

et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.  
and there are those that must be pierced when they are ripe, and do not mature according to their completion, such as abscesses near the joints.  

Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.  
For when abscesses form near joints, and they are left until they decay around them, the ligaments and nerves of the joint may become damaged, which causes contraction in that limb.  

Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;  
Or the abscess is near a vital organ, and if you delay the piercing until it is mature, it will harm the vital organ;  

ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;  
or it is near the base, and it must be pierced before it matures;  

et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;  
and you must not pierce a ripe abscess without completed digestion, except for one near the base, so that it does not rot deeply, spread within, and form a fistula;  

et ne puisse saner en grant termine.  
and it cannot heal for a long time.  

Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;  
And you must know the proper time to pierce an abscess that is mature according to its completion, which is when the pain has subsided, the fever has diminished, the pain and redness have lessened, along with the swelling and hardening at the head of the abscess, and the other signs;  

et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;  
and you must place the piercing at the lowest point of the abscess, where it appears most swollen;  

et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.  
and the piercing should align with the body’s length, whether the abscess is on the hands or feet, or near joints, nerves, and arteries, and in all places where there is no curvature.  

En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.  
In those that curve, according to the contour of that limb.  

Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.  
And when the abscess is in a fleshy area, it is better to wait for the piercing until it is established with completed digestion, as we have said.  

Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;  
For if you pierce it before that, the body will be spread with its venom and filled with much filth;  

et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.  
and perhaps its edges and depth will harden.  

Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.  
And there are some abscesses that are pierced across the breadth of the body, according to what the limbs require.  

Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;  
And you must administer small openings for small abscesses;  

et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;  
and for large abscesses, large openings, and multiple cuts according to the size of the abscess;  

et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;  
and there are abscesses where the core must be exposed and cut;  

quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:  
when it has already become like a strip of cloth and is lifeless, it must be treated as one does with carbuncles:  

et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;  
and there are some that are split into three angles, and others that are cut like the leaf of myrtle, such as abscesses of boils;  

et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.  
and there are others where a round incision is made, and other cuts and similar shapes.  

Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;  
Those that have no head, such as soft superficial abscesses, must be pierced fully;  

et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;  
and when the abscess is large and has accumulated much pus, and you pierce it, you must not extract all the pus at once, but only a part;  

puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;  
then plug the abscess until the next day, then extract some more again;  

fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;  
do this many times, little by little, until all the pus is expelled;  

meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.  
especially if the patient is of weak strength, a pregnant woman, a small child, or an elderly decrepit man.  

Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.  
For the spirit sometimes departs with the expulsion of the pus, and the patient may die without you noticing.  

Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;  
Avoid, therefore, this step with great caution, and when you have pierced the abscess, wipe the wound and check if the abscess wound is small;  

et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;  
and if it is a full incision, administer linen or old cotton wicks;  

et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;  
and if it is a large abscess with many openings, you must place a wick in each one so they meet each other;  

et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;  
and if you have cut part of the skin in the abscess and exposed it around, you must fill it with old cotton or scraps of linen without moisture, and bind it until the third day;  

puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then remove it, and treat it with ointment until it is healed.  

Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.  
And if a flow of blood occurs during your procedure, administer cold water and vinegar, soak a cloth, and place it over the bleeding area several times.  

Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;  
And if the flow of blood persists, apply care and management, and use the powders I have mentioned in various places in this book; and if it is winter, and the area or the abscess is very sensitive, you must apply tents and cloths soaked in hot wine and oil.  

Et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;  
And if it is summer, and the area is fleshy, you must apply cloths soaked in water and oil, or in cold wine and oil, until the third day, as we have said.  

Et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then open the abscess, clean and treat it as required, until it is healed.  

Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:  
And this must be universally understood in the treatment of abscesses:  

Or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.  
Now I have told you how to proceed with the treatment of abscesses, and here is the chapter.  

Des soros  
Of sores  

Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.  
On the surface of the head, small abscesses appear, and they are like knots in cloth, resembling the yolk of an egg, with many similar forms.  

Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;  
Some are fatty, and some have moisture like pus.  

Et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.  
And there are some that are hard and stony when cut, and there is no doubt unless the artery is affected.  

Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.  
And the process of cutting requires that you test with an instrument called a "trocar," the shape of which is described below, to determine what it contains.  

Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.  
For if it contains moisture, you make an incision lengthwise above it.  

Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;  
And when the moisture has been emptied, scrape without leaving any of the skin that held that moisture, for it will return if anything is left behind.  

Puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;  
Then dip cotton in Egyptian ointment, if it is available.  

Se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;  
If not, in water and salt, and use it to fill the wound, leaving it until the next day.  

Et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.  
And this will expel what remained overnight.  

Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;  
And then repeat the cotton treatment, as before, on the second and third day, until you are sure nothing remains from the night.  

Puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then treat the wound with suitable ointments until it is healed.  

Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;  
And if the abscess contains fatty matter, cut it in this form, lengthwise.  

Et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;  
And apply your ointments, scrape it from all sides, and focus your care on removing the layer where it lies.  

Et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.  
And if the artery causes you trouble, do what I have told you later.  

Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.  
And do the same for the abscess if it is stony, cutting and treating it as I have instructed.  

Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.  
And cutting a stony or moist abscess is easier, as they contain little blood.  

Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;  
And there are some abscesses on the head with no moisture, such as one I cut from the head of an old woman.  

Et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;  
And I found the abscess to be like a heavy stone, rough and white, and it could not be broken.  

Et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.  
And if one struck it, it would cause a wound as if from a stone.  

En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;  
In other abscesses appearing on the head, except those that arise on children’s heads or near the roots of the ears, the incision must always be made at the lowest point to let the pus flow out.  

Et les cure si com il covient.  
And treat them as required.  

des scrophules  
Of the scrofula.  

Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.  
Many times, these abscesses occur on the neck, under the armpits, and in the groin, and sometimes appear elsewhere on the body; they are numerous and often interconnected.  

Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;  
And each scrofula is properly contained within its own layer, like the swellings and abscesses of the head, as we have mentioned.  

et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.  
And the appearances of these scrofula are many.  

Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.  
There are some that contain moisture, and there are malignant ones that refuse to heal.  

en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;  
In those that you see are well-disposed to the touch, resembling the color of the body, movable in all directions, and not connected to the nerves of the neck, nor to the artery, nor to the conduit, and are not deep;  

si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;  
Then you must cut it from above, and peel it from all sides, and stretch the two lips of the wound with hooks, if you need them, as we have said about abscesses of the head.  

et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.  
And remove it little by little, being sure not to cut the nerve or the vein, and ensure that the knife is neither too sharp nor too cutting, so that the hand does not slip or go too far, to avoid cutting what should not be cut.  

Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;  
And if you cut the vein or the artery, and this prevents you from working, apply crushed vitriol or some powders that staunch blood, and compress the wound.  

et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.  
And leave it until the abscess subsides, the wound softens, and begins to suppurate.  

Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;  
And when the bleeding has stopped, return to your work until it is completed.  

puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.  
Then, use your index finger to check if any small scrofula remain, and if so, cut and clean them.  

Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;  
And if there is a large vein at the root of the scrofula, you must not cut the scrofula at its root but tie it with a strong double thread and let it fall off on its own without causing harm.  

puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.  
Then fill the wound with old cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment, and treat it.  

Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.  
And if you cut out the entire scrofula, you must bring together the two lips of the wound, sew them immediately, ensuring there is no excess flesh remaining due to the size of the scrofula.  

si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.  
You must ensure to cut its root, extract it fully, and sew it as we have described.  

Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;  
Those scrofula that contain excess fluid should be pierced where they appear ripe.  

et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;  
Pierce it as described earlier, depending on its state, then administer wicks with ointment and similar substances so that it destroys what remains of the corruption.  

et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
And when the wound is well cleaned, treat it with ointments that regenerate flesh until it heals.  

de squinance  
Of quinsy.  

Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;  
The ancients spoke and wrote about the incision of the throat.  

mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.  
But I have never seen anyone in our land perform it, and these are the writings of their words.  

A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;  
For those who have quinsy, it is necessary that the opening in the throat, called the "epiglottis," be cut.  

et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.  
And help is not made through this because all the veins and lungs of the patient are affected when they have a hot abscess in the mouth, the throat, or the tonsils.  

Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.  
When the illness is in the channel of the lungs, it is necessary to cut the epiglottis to prevent the death caused by strangulation.  

Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;  
Therefore, when we want to split the epiglottis, we must make a small transverse incision under the third or fourth ring, between the two rings, or to the extent of the incision in the membrane, but not into the cartilage.  

et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.  
And this spot is suitable for the section of the epiglottis because there is no flesh there, and the vessels are distant.  

Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;  
And if the practitioner is hesitant, he must stretch the skin of the throat with a hook, then cut the tissue until he reaches the channel.  

et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;  
And avoid the blood vessels if you see any, and then cut the membrane, as we have described.  

et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;  
And the cutting is evident by the discharge of phlegm from the channel that escapes through the broken area and by the loss of voice.  

et laisse la plaie overte une piece.  
And leave the wound open for a while.  

Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;  
And when the time has passed during which one fears strangulation, bring together the two lips of the wound of the heart, and sew it entirely without the cartilage;  

puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then administer medicines that cause flesh to grow, until it is healed.  

Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.  
Albucasim says that this should not be done until the throat is completely obstructed, and the patient is judged to be dying, and breath fails him.  

Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;  
Then one cuts the epiglottis because the patient cannot breathe, and he breathes through the wound, and thus is saved from death;  

et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII. Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;  
and for this, the ancients recommended leaving the wound open until the severity of the illness has passed, which occurs in three or four days.  Then they recommended sewing the wound and treating it until it was healed;  

et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.  
and I will tell you what I saw.  

Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;  
I saw a young woman take a knife, drive it into her throat, and cut part of the bronchial tubes;  

et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.  
and I was called to treat her, and I found her as if dead.  

Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.  
I uncovered the wound, and found the blood that had flowed from it, and I knew well that she had cut neither a vein nor a vessel other than the throat, and the air was escaping through the wound.  

Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;  
I hastened, and sewed the wound, and treated it until it was healed;  

et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;  
and nothing happened to the young woman except that her voice was hoarse, and she later returned to her normal state;  

por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.  
therefore, I say that one should not fear the cutting of the epiglottis.  

de la grosse gorge  
On the large throat  

Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;  
This swelling is called "hernia of the throat," and it is a large swelling, the color of a jasper, and is very common in women;  

et est selonc II manieres:  
and it occurs in two forms:  

naturez, et accidens;  
natural, and accidental;  

ou natureil n’a point d’engien.  
the natural one has no remedy.  

Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;  
And the accidental one is of two kinds, one resembling fatty nodes, and the other resembling a swelling that comes from a node of an artery;  

et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:  
and there is fear, and one should only operate on the small ones, testing and probing it with the introducer:  

se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;  
if you find it like a fatty node, and it is not attached to any vein, then cut it as one cuts nodes, and remove it with its covering, if it has one;  

et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.  
and examine everything well, and treat it as is necessary, until it is completely healed.  

des nous  
On nodes  

Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;  
There are many kinds of nodes, of which I will describe all the forms;  

et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.  
and now I must explain all the differences between a node and a discharge.  

Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;  
I say that a discharge involves heat and accompanying fever, until the inflammation subsides, and the putrefaction is complete;  

adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.  
then the fever and the heat cease.  

Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;  
With a node, there is neither heat, fever, nor pain, and it contains a membrane, which is its own sac and is the color of the body, beginning like a jasper, and becoming large;  

et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.  
and they are of two types, either fatty or moist, and of many colors, as I mentioned in the classification.  

Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.  
It is necessary, when you come to the treatment of a node, to test and examine it first with the instrument called the “introducer,” as its form will be explained in the following chapter.  

Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;  
And the method of examining swellings of the nodes is to take the moistest part you find in the swelling, and rotate your fingers little by little, until you know that the instrument has pierced the core, according to the size of the swelling;  

puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.  
then remove the introducer, and observe what flows out.  

Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;  
If flowing moisture runs out, note its color, and incise it as I described for other swellings;  

et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;  
and if no moisture comes out after the introducer, know that it is fatty, so cut it in a cross, take it with pincers, and gently strip it on each side, and ensure the coat where it lies is extracted intact with the node;  

et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.  
and if you cannot extract it intact, then remove it piece by piece until nothing remains.  

Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;  
For if anything remains, the node will return many times;  

et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;  
and if a little remains, and the blood troubles you, fill the wound with some sharp corrosive powders, compress the wound, and apply soothing poultices to the swelling, and treat it with other remedies until it is healed;  

et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.  
and if the node is large, sew the two lips of the wound and treat it with what generates flesh.  

et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;  
and if the beating vein or something else troubles you, hurry and fill the area with crushed vitriol, and leave it covered for two or three days, until the wound festers and the blood's inflammation subsides;  

puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.  
then return to cutting away what remains of the node.  

Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:  
Here are the forms of introducer instruments, and they are of three types:  

grans et moien et petit;  
large, medium, and small;  

et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:  
and there are three square ones called "albaret," and one called "breb," and these come in three types:  

grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;  
large, medium, and small, for examining fistula swellings;  

et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;  
and they are like the needles used to sew tendons, and they are made of yellow brass, or iron, or silver, and those of yellow brass are preferable, and black lead is better tested for probing the curves of fistulas;  

et sont de III manieres:  
and they are of three types:  

grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.  
large, medium, and small, according to the size of the opening.  

Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:  
The forms of hooks are of many types, as you see here:  

grans, moiens, et petis;  
large, medium, and small;  

et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;  
and there are hooks with two curves of three types as well;  

et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;  
and there are hooks with three curves, and these also come in three types;  

et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;  
and there are hooks with two curves, and hooks with only one curve, and these come in three types;  

et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.  
and all of these are necessary for their respective uses.  

Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;  
The heads of those used for cutting are sharp, and there are some that cut only on one side, with which nodes are stripped, to avoid cutting veins or nerves;  

et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;  
and some of these introducers have blades set in handles, so the patient does not notice during the opening of swellings;  

et sont de III manieres:  
and they are of three types:  

grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;  
large, small, and medium, as you see;  

et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;  
and they are used only on fleshy areas, such as the legs, arms, breasts, groin, and similar places;  

et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:  
and sometimes one makes another small instrument, resembling pistachio shells, in this form, used to stop bleeding:  

et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:  
and it is sometimes placed on the area bleeding from the cutting of veins and arteries, and sometimes it is used in this larger form:  

Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;  
Sometimes the breasts of some men swell when they begin to become corrupted, until they resemble women's breasts;  

et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:  
and they remain unsightly and swollen, and anyone who wishes to treat them must incise them following this form from line .b. to line .g.:  

puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;  
then strip the fat, fill the wound with medicine that generates flesh, then bring together the two lips of the wound with stitching, and treat it until it is healed;  

et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;  
and if the breast slopes downward and is softened due to its size, as happens with women, make two incisions on the top, with two similar cuts;  

de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;  
one of which should meet the other at the ends, so that the larger line contains the smaller one, following this form, from line .b. to line .g.;
