puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;  
then strip the skin between the two lips, remove the fat, and apply what we have mentioned about stitching and powders, and what is necessary for the treatment, until it is healed;  

et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;  
and if it does not heal, or the incision is not completely made because the patient refuses to rest, or because of the flow of blood, you must fill the wound with cotton soaked in a corrosive ointment;  

et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.  
and leave it until it consumes the remainder and the fat, then treat it until it is healed.  

des apostemes des asselles  
Of abscesses of the armpits  

Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.  
These abscesses that arise under the armpits are types of hard scrofula with ridges, and there are some that contain moisture.  

Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:  
Thus, those that contain moisture must be cut in this manner, from line .b. to line .g.:  

Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.  
And when all the pus that is in the abscess is emptied, fill the wound with old cotton, and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton, and treat it with an appropriate ointment until it is healed.  

Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.  
And if the abscess resembles scrofula, cut it as we have explained in the incisions for scrofula, and if the wound releases pus, apply cauterization as we have described earlier.  

de la routure de l’artere  
Of the rupture of the artery  

Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;  
When the artery is ruptured, and the skin above it is closed, abscesses often form, and the same happens with a swollen and abscessed vein.  

et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;  
And it can be recognized when it is due to the artery, as the abscess is long and deep.  

et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;  
And when you feel it with your fingers, you sense a constriction.  

et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;  
And when it is due to the vein, there are apparent red streaks.  

et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.  
And it is folly to cut this abscess, especially when it is under the armpits, in the groin, on the neck, or in many other places, and it is very large.  

Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;  
Thus, one must avoid using a knife for treatment, and this must also be avoided for one at the head, while for one caused by artery swelling, cut along the skin lengthwise.  

puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;  
Then open the incision with hooks, and carefully separate the artery from the tissues until it is exposed.  

puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;  
Then insert a needle beneath it, and pierce it through to the other side, and tie the artery tightly in two places with a double thread, as I have instructed you in the extraction of the two arteries in the temples.  

puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;  
Then pierce the area between the two ties with a trocar until the blood contained therein is released, and the abscess is emptied.  

puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;  
Then apply the treatment that prevents the generation of pus, until the ties fall off.  

puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;  
Then treat it with an appropriate ointment until it is healed.  

et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;  
And if the abscess is due to the incision of the vein, you must grasp with your hand as much of the abscess and skin as you can, then insert the needle under the area you are holding, and pierce it, passing through a double thread so that it comes out on the other side.  

puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;  
Then tie the abscess, as I have told you, with a tie at one of the two ends of the thread.  

et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;  
And if you fear that the thread may come loose, insert another needle with a thread beneath the entire abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tighten the threads in four places.  

puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;  
Then cut the abscess so that the excess flows out, then cut the excess from the core and leave what is tied.  

puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then place a small cloth moistened with wine and oil on it, and administer treatments with wicks and ointments until it is healed.  

des apostemes des ners  
Of abscesses of the nerves  

Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.  
Just as abscesses occur in arteries and veins, abscesses occur in nerves when they are injured, or from excessive strain, and similar causes.  

Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;  
And this happens more often in the wrists, fingers, and in all places with joints, and it is a serious abscess, and its color resembles the color of the body, and it is in many cases without pain.  

et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;  
And when it is pressed firmly, the patient feels pain, and it is not deep within the body but beneath the skin.  

et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:  
And it moves easily in all directions and does not go forward or backward, nor below nor above, and the one that is in joints must not be cut with a knife.  

par aventure i vanroit contraction;  
For contraction could result.  

et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.  
And for one that is in the head or forehead, cut the skin with a spatula.  

Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;  
If the abscess is small, hold it with forceps and cut it at its root.  

et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
And if it is large, suspend it with a hook, skin it, then remove it and close the wound with sutures, and treat it until it is healed.  

des grosses boces pendans  
Of large hanging lumps  

Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;  
Sometimes it occurs on the belly and nowhere else, this "fungus," and it is a condition called "funge" because of its resemblance to mushrooms, with thin roots and a large head.  

et en i a de petis et de mout grans;  
And there are small ones and very large ones.  

et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.  
And I saw a man who had two on his belly that resembled mushrooms more than anything else, and there was no difference between them; they were white, had fine roots, were already split, and constantly oozed moisture.  

Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;  
I cut them and found that one weighed eighteen ounces, and the other six; and the procedure in the incision is such that you must observe whether the growth is moist, and whether the color of the lump is white, moist, and has fine roots.  

si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.  
Cut it with a broad spatula, and have the cautery heated in the fire ready before you.  

Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;  
For during the cutting, there often comes too great a flow of blood, and if the bleeding overwhelms you, hasten to cauterize it.  

et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;  
And if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the incision with the knife, take a well-made lead thread, tie it around the lump as we have described, and leave it for two days.  

et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;  
Then tighten it further, and continue tightening the lead thread until it cuts through the lump, which will fall off on its own without effort.  

et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;  
And if the roots are thick, cutting is dangerous, especially on the belly, but you can cut half of it and then cauterize it to prevent regrowth.  

puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.  
Then treat the wound, and be careful not to cut the lump that is of a pale color, poor consistency, and unhealthy appearance.  

Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.  
For it is a cancerous abscess, and I will address the treatment of cancer later.  

quant li boude ist fuer  
When the bowel protrudes  

Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;  
If the appearance of the bowel is caused by cautery of a wound or splitting of the diaphragm, and it is on the belly and some of the bowels protrude, as happens in other ruptures, or from blood flowing from veins or arteries as previously mentioned, or from air pressure;  

et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.  
And if it is from the rupture of the diaphragm and the escape of the bowel, the color of the abscess resembles the color of the body, it is a light condition without pain, and presents with varied discharge.  

Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.  
And if it is due to the escape of the intestine, it is more variable, and when pressed with the fingers, it retreats, then returns, and sometimes it becomes constricted and grows significantly when entering a bath or after great exertion.  

Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;  
And if it is due to moisture, it is a light condition and is evident when pressed by hand, without much resistance.  

et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;  
And if it is due to blood, the abscess appears large and hard, and is confined to a specific area.  

et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.  
And if it is due to air pressure, it is soft to the touch, and the procedure is to determine if the appearance is caused by arterial blood, venous blood, or air pressure.  

Si covient que tu laisses la cure.  
Then you must abandon the treatment.  

Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.  
For he has doubt and fear, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, because of the artery and the vein.  

Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;  
And if the manifestation is in the intestine or the bowel, you must command the patient to hold their breath, lie fully stretched, then cut around the navel.  

puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;  
Then order them to lie frequently under your hands, go around the area you have marked with the spatula, and lift half the abscess above with the large hook.  

puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;  
Then tie it tightly with a strong thread or a cord of durable silk, and secure the knot firmly.  

puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;  
Then open the half of the abscess stretched over the binding, insert your index finger, and search for the intestine.  

se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;  
If you find it caught in the binding, untie it and push the intestine back outside the abdomen.  

et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;  
If you find the bowel, take it with the hook and cut off the excess.  

et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;  
If the artery or vein resists, proceed carefully around it, then return to your work and take two needles with two strong threads, passing the needles around the area you crossed and pierced.  

puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;  
Then tighten the abscess in four places above the needles, and if you wish, remove the needles and leave the site until it rots and the dead flesh falls off by itself.  

ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;  
Or cut it when it becomes softened and rotten, then treat the site as necessary, and finish with the abscess as we have described.  

et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.  
Extract the blood or moisture you find, then treat the site as needed and close the wound.  

dou chancre  
On the chancre  

Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;  
We have discussed in the classification the types of chancre, how to treat it with medicines, and how to avoid surgical intervention.  

et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;  
We mention the chancre that arises in the womb, requiring great caution in treatment, and the ancients said that when a chancre is in a place where it can be removed, such as the breast, the thigh, or similar areas, it should be completely excised at the onset.  

et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;  
And when it is large and old, you must not approach it, for I was never able to cure one.  

ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.  
Nor did anyone before me ever cure one.  

Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;  
And the procedure, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you purge the patient sometimes of black bile;  

puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;  
then bleed him if he has evident repletion, then place the patient in a good position to perform the procedure;  

puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;  
then throw out the ulcers or chancre, and the flesh from all sides, and remove it from all sides without leaving anything behind;  

et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;  
and let the blood flow completely, and press the area firmly with your hand or with something else, and if the flow of blood opposes you due to the incision in the artery or vein, then cauterize it until the blood is stopped;  

puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.  

de ydropisie  
on dropsy  

Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:  
We have already spoken in the division about the types of dropsy, and how the gathering of fluid is formed, and the signs of each type, and the treatment done with medicines, and that which is cured by the knife:  

si est eclites soulement;  
this concerns ascites alone;  

et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:  
and one must not touch these two types with a knife:  

c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;  
namely, tympanites and hypochondriac dropsy, for they are fatal conditions;  

donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;  
therefore, when you treat this form of dropsy called "ascites" with medicines, and the treatment does not help, then observe whether the patient is weak, or if he has another disease besides dropsy, such as fever and diarrhea and similar conditions;  

si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;  
then do not touch him with a knife, for there is risk;  

et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:  
but if you see that the patient is of strong constitution, and he has no other illness but dropsy alone, and he is neither too young nor too old, then you should proceed in this way:  

lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:  
lift the patient upright with your hands, and the assistant presses the belly, pushing the fluid toward the lowest part of the abdomen, then take the spined spatula in this shape:  

Et soit trenchans de II pars.  
And let it be sharp on both sides.  

a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;  
with a point, and yet not so penetrating that it can reach the intestines when it is inserted, and cannot injure them;  

puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:  
then observe whether the dropsy is situated near the intestines:  

si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;  
then it is necessary to cut above the navel, three finger-widths directly below the sternum;  

et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;  
and if the dropsy is due to a disease of the liver, then let your incision be on the left of the navel, three finger-widths away;  

et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;  
and if it is due to the spleen, then let it be on the right, and the patient must not lie on the incision so that the superfluities do not flow to that weak spot;  

puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;  
then pierce all the skin with the instrument, and insert it, and lift your hand with the spatula between the skin and the membrane as if skinning, to the extent of a fingernail or slightly around it;  

puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:  
then pierce the membrane until the spatula reaches the empty space, which is the place of the fluid, then withdraw it and insert this instrument, whose shape is as follows:  

Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;  
It resembles a thin silver reed and is made of light brass or copper, and has a small opening at the lower part;  

et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;  
and on one side, three openings;  

et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;  
and two on the other side, and one elsewhere;  

et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:  
and its head is shaped like a quill, in the form of the incision that a scribe makes on a pen;  

au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;  
at the upper end is the little ring, so that when the instrument reaches the fluid, it descends immediately into the tool;  

vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;  
then drain half or a third of it, for if you drain more than necessary at that time, by chance the patient may die from the dissolution of his spirit, or he may faint, or approach death;  

mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;  
but drain according to the quantity of his strength and according to what the dispositions of the patient’s vitality and his pulse signify;  

puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;  
then withdraw the instrument and retain the fluid, and it is retained immediately by the plug that stops the opening in the membrane, of which I have spoken, that you pierce in this manner;  

puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;  
then use the instrument again on another day, if you see the patient enduring this well, and draw out a small quantity of fluid;  

fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.  
do this for several days, and be careful not to err so that only a little fluid remains.  

Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;  
And if you have doubts about the patient, and you leave a lot of fluid, then treat him with burial in hot sand, and with much sweating or baths and exposure to the sun, and limit his drinking;  

et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.  
and treat him with drying medicines until he is healed, and cauterize over the stomach, the liver, and the spleen after the extraction of the fluid, as I have mentioned before.  

de l’estopement de la verge  
On the obstruction of the penis  

Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.  
Sometimes children are born without an opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place.  

Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:  
It is necessary immediately to pierce it with a very fine spatula in the following shape:  

puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;  
then insert into the opening a small fine lead tube, bind it, and leave it thus for three or four days; and when he wants to urinate, remove the tube, let him urinate, and then reinsert it;  

et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.  
and perhaps this is not needed, for the urine that comes out prevents it from closing.  

Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.  
For those whose opening is small, it should be treated with the lead tube, as we have said, and it will widen.  

Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;  
Those whose opening is not in its proper place are injured, for some are born with the opening at the tip of the penis, which prevents them from urinating forward unless they lift their penis upward;  

et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.  
and they cannot procreate because the substance cannot reach the womb, and this is a grave condition.  

Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;  
And the method of the procedure is that the patient lies often on his back, then the tip of the penis is extended and cut like the shaping of a quill, so that the opening is in the middle, as it should be;  

et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and beware of the flow of blood that often occurs, and if it does, stop it with something that stops bleeding, and treat the wound until it is healed.  

des pustules de la verge  
On pustules of the penis  

Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;  
Many times, these pustules appear on the penis, and it is an appearance of unsightly flesh;  

et en i a malignes et non malignes;  
and there are malignant and non-malignant ones;  

si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;  
you must take them with a fine hook, cut and clean them all, then apply cotton moistened with Egyptian ointment;  

puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then treat it with diafinicon ointment until it is healed.  

Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.  
And if the pustule is malignant, of foul color and smell, it is necessary to apply cautery.  

Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;  
When you have cut it, and if the pustule is at the top of the penis and partly under the skin and partly outside, you must first remove the part of the pustule that is inside;  

et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.  
and when it is healed, treat the outer part.  

Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;  
For if you treat both together, the tip of the penis is not secure from being pierced, and blackening and corruption will occur in the penis and the testicles;  

si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  
thus it is necessary to remove all that is black and corrupted, then apply a plaster of honey and flour made from pomegranate peel and vetch, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.  

Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:  
And if a flow of blood occurs, apply the lunar cautery in the following way:  

Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:  
The cautery assists in two conditions at once:  

c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;  
namely, the flow of blood and the corruption;  

et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;  
and if the tip of the penis is corrupted and constricted, it is necessary to insert a lead reed into the canal of the penis, and the patient urinates through it;  

et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;  
and when the skin tightens at the tip of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or it occurs from a wound or abscess, it is necessary to free it with a sharp instrument, so that the binding is undone, and the tip of the penis is freed from all sides;  

et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;  
and if it is a severe matter to resolve, it is necessary to free it slightly with a spatula from the tip of the penis and the skin;  

puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.  
then carefully separate the two, and insert a small fine linen cloth moistened with cold water so that it does not tighten again.  

de la circoncision  
Of circumcision  

Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;  
Circumcision is not a rupture of continuity like other wounds;  

toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.  
however, when we perform this act voluntarily, especially on children, it is necessary that we do it in the best and safest manner for their well-being.  

Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.  
I say that the ancients did not speak of circumcision for their children, for it was not practiced in their law, and we only have what we have learned through experience.  

Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;  
For I have seen the majority of masters and practitioners perform circumcision with a knife, with forceps, and with a razor;  

si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.  
and the flesh would retract because there are two layers, and sometimes the one above is cut while the one below remains.  

Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;  
Then it must be cut again, and the pain is doubled, and in the healing of the wound from the knife, the edge of the member is not securely treated;  

et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.  
and with the healing by the nail, sometimes the flesh slips, and the work fails, and many times they grow in such a way that no further healing is needed, and I have seen this.  

De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.  
In the healing done with forceps and a binding thread, I have found the effectiveness of this method, for the forceps cut precisely both above and below.  

Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;  
For when you press your hand, you cut evenly in one single motion;  

mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;  
but ensure that the thread is tightly wrapped around the skin;  

et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;  
and the method of the initial work should be that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around the member, and you can distract him in every way possible;  

puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;  
then have him stand straight between your hands, and conceal the forceps in your hands or beneath your feet so the child does not see them or any of the instruments;  

puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;  
then place your hand on the member, blow on the flesh, and pull it up so that the head of the member is visible;  

puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;  
then clean it thoroughly of the filth that has accumulated there, then tie the spot firmly with a double thread, and tie it below with another binding a little apart;  

et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;  
and hold it with two fingers by the second binding, with the thumb and forefinger, and cut between the two bindings, then quickly remove the upper flesh and pull the head of the member;  

puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;  
then let the blood flow little by little, for it is cleansing;  

et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and apply powder, and on the powder place a small piece of soft linen moistened with a mixture of cooked egg yolk, rose water, and good, fresh rose oil, and leave it on until the next day, and care for it with other treatments until it heals.  

Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:  
The shape of the forceps for the healing is as follows:  

li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:  
the two ends should be slender and sharp, and the heads should be as large as the handle, evenly so:  

li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;  
the error in the healing occurs when the inner flesh retracts during the incision;  

donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;  
then you must extend it with your nail, before the site becomes infected;  

et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.  
and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your nail, hold it with pincers and then cut it.  

Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;  
And if three days pass and the flesh beneath the member becomes swollen, leave it until the swelling subsides, and then gently scrape it;  

si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.  
then cut it as best as you can without damaging the member, for this will not harm it.  

Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;  
Treat the site with soothing powders, as we have mentioned in the treatise on powders, and if the flesh is cut beyond measure and extends above, it will not harm it;  

cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
therefore, treat it as we have said, until it is healed.  

dou retenement de l’urine  
Of the retention of urine  

Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;  
The retention of urine is caused by the obstruction of a stone, coagulated blood, pus, flesh growth, or similar things, as we have mentioned in the division;  

et se li urine n’est desliie, et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;  
and if the urine is not released, and you see that the retention is due to a stone lodged in the neck of the bladder, the patient should kneel and bend forward;  

et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;  
and their feet should be placed on their back, the belly stretched upward from the back, and the patient should hold their breath as much as they can;  

et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie;  
then the neck of the bladder is compressed to expel the stone, which allows the urine to be released;  

et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:  
and if it does not flow as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, you must administer extraction with the instrument called a "syringe," the shape of which is as follows:  

et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;  
it should be made of fine silver, lightweight, and smooth, like the feather of a bird;  

et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.  
and the shaft should be one and a half palms long, and the tip should be thin.  

Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;  
The method for releasing the urine is as follows: take a double thread, tie a small amount of wool or cotton to the end, and place the end of the thread into the syringe;  

et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;  
cut away the excess wool and push it to the tip of the syringe, then coat the syringe with oil, butter, or egg white, and have the patient sit on a seat, and anoint the bladder and the penis with moist oil, olive oil, and warm water;  

puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;  
then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches its root, and bend the penis over towards the bow;  

puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;  
then push the syringe further until it reaches the bladder, and the patient will feel it come to the empty cavity, and this is done only when the passage it enters is twisted;  

puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;  
then slowly extend the thread along with the wool, and the urine will follow the wool, then remove it, and let the urine flow;  

et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.  
and repeat with the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and the patient is relieved.  

des maladies de la vessie  
Of the diseases of the bladder  

Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:  
When abrasions or blood appear in the bladder, or rot has accumulated there, and you wish to distill waters or medicines into it, use the instrument called a "clepsydra," the shape of which is as follows:  

Elle est close, et si a III pertus:  
It is closed and has three openings:  

II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;  
two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;  

et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;  
and the terminal opening through which the medicine flows should seal the penis well without addition, so that moisture can be drawn out and pushed in as needed;  

et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;  
and when you want to send your medicines into the bladder, place the head of the clepsydra in the moisture, and pull on the plunger inside;  

si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;  
then you will draw the moisture into the clepsydra, and then push the plunger firmly back in;  

si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;  
then the moisture will enter and go into the bladder immediately, so that the patient will feel it;  

et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:  
and this is the form of the delicate clyster used to irrigate the bladder:  

si est ci:  
It is as follows:  

Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;  
It is made of silver or brass, and its head is higher;  

et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;  
and below, it has a ring where the bindings attach;  

puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;  
then take a sheep’s bladder and place in it the moisture with which you want to irrigate the bladder, then tie it between the two rings firmly with a good double thread, and warm the moisture slightly over the fire;  

puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;  
then insert the head of the clyster into the penis, and press your hand gently on the bladder along with the moisture until the patient feels that the moisture has already entered the bladder;  

et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;  
and if you do not have the bladder, take a piece of parchment, make a circle, and pierce it roundly around;  

puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;  
then thread a strong string through these holes, assemble the circle as one assembles a ring, and place inside it the oil, moisture, and water you wish, and attach it to the instrument;  

et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.  
and do as you would with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.  

de la piere  
Of the stone  

Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;  
We have already spoken in the section about the types of stones and their extraction along with medicines;  

et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;  
and I have explained the difference between the stone formed in the kidneys, all the signs, and the cases in which a stone should be operated on by incision;  

et en la vessie, et en la verge;  
and in the bladder, and in the penis;  

et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.  
and I will explain it to you clearly and briefly.  

Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;  
I say that the stone formed in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign when urine flows from the bladder resembling water in its fineness;  

et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;  
and sand appears in it, and the patient rubs his penis, which often droops, and then stiffens;  

et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;  
and many times their anus discharges;  

et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;  
and healing is easy in children up to four years old, very difficult in the elderly, and moderate in the young, those between youth and old age;  

et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.  
and treatment is easier for those who have a large stone than for those who have a small one.  

Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.  
And when we proceed to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with an enema to remove all the feces from the intestines.  

Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.  
For it sometimes hinders the search for the stone.  

Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;  
Then take the patient by the feet, lift him up and shake him below, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder and sometimes dislodges from its high position;  

puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;  
then seat him between your prepared hands, his hands placed under his thighs, so that the bladder is entirely inclined downward;  

puis la quier et la touche dedens;  
then search for and touch the stone within;  

se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.  
if you feel the stone in the space, hasten now to incise above the stone.  

Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;  
And if it does not completely descend when touched, moisten your index finger with oil from your left hand if the patient is a child, or your middle finger if the patient is a young adult;  

et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;  
insert it into his anus, search for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, guide it to the neck of the bladder;  

puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.  
then press with your finger and push it outward to where you want to incise.  

Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;  
And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and to extend the testicles upward with his right hand, while with his left hand removing the skin beneath the testicles in the area where the incision is to be made;  

puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:  
then insert the cutting spatumile, the form of which is this:  

Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;  
And make an incision between the area between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but toward the left buttock;  

et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;  
and make it directly over the stone, keeping your fingers in the anus, and the incision should be transverse, wide on the outside and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, but not too large;  

par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;  
perhaps press with the finger in the anus, so that it comes out easily without effort;  

et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:  
and know that there are some stones with angles and edges:  

si est griés a issir;  
they are difficult to extract;  

et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.  
and there are others that are smooth, resembling an acorn, and round, for which extraction is easier.  

A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;  
For those with angles and edges, make the incision larger;  

et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;  
and if it does not come out, you must use tongs shaped like a file at the tip to tightly grasp the stone so that it does not slip;  

ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;  
or you insert beneath it a delicate instrument curved at the tip;  

et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;  
and if you cannot maneuver it this way, widen the opening a bit, and if bleeding occurs, staunch it with vitriol;  

et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.  
and if there is more than one stone, first bring the largest one to the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, extract it, and then the smaller ones if there are several.  

Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.  
And if it is very large, it must be broken, and a larger incision must be made.  

Car II choses avienent au malaide:  
For two things happen to the patient:  

ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;  
either he dies, or the urine continuously leaks because the wound cannot heal;  

mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;  
but nevertheless, strive to remove it, or break it with pliers, until you extract it piece by piece;  

et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;  
and when you have completed your work, fill the wound with incense, aloe, and dragon's blood, compress it, and place over it a cloth moistened with oil and wine, or with oil, rose water, and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess;  

puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.  
then recline the patient on his back and do not untie the bandage until the third day.  

Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
And when you untie it, thoroughly moisten the area with oil and water, then treat it with dyafinicon ointment and basilicon ointment until it is healed.  

Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:  
And if hot abscesses appear in the wound, along with erosions and blood clots in the bladder, and this causes urine retention, which is mixed with blood in such a way that it flows together with the urine:  

boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;  
then insert your finger into the wound and extract the blood, for if it remains, it will spread through the bladder and corrupt it;  

puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;  
then wash the wound with water, garlic, and salt, and treat it in every way you know until it is healed;  

et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.  
and each time you treat him, it is necessary to bind his thighs together and apply the medicines to the affected area.  

Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;  
And if the stone is small, lodged in the urethral passage, and prevents urine from flowing out;  

si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.  
then treat it as I mentioned earlier, cutting it several times if necessary; in this way, you are excused from performing a more invasive procedure.  

Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.  
I have already proven this method in practice.  

Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:  
Take an iron drill shaped like this, with three edges fixed to a shaft:  

puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;  
then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot move back into the bladder;  

puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;  
then gently insert the drill into the urethra until it reaches the stone;  

et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;  
and rotate the drill with your hand little by little on the stone until you can pierce through it;  

si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.  
then the urine will flow immediately; next, press your hand on the remaining part of the stone that is still inside the urethra.  

Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;  
It will soon break, and the fragments will pass out with the urine, and the patient will be healed;  

et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;  
and if for some reason you cannot do this, tie one thread below the stone and another above it, then cut the urethra at the level of the stone between the two ligatures, extract the stone, untie the ligature, and clean the clotted blood from the wound;  

et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and treat it until it is healed.  

de la piere des femmes  
About the stone in women  

Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:  
It seldom happens that a stone forms in women, and if it does, the treatment is difficult and hindered for three reasons:  

l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;  
the first is that the woman might be a virgin;  

et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.  
and the second is that it is difficult to find a knowledgeable woman willing to expose herself to physicians, especially when she is chaste.  

Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;  
And the third reason is that it is difficult to find a woman skilled in this art with her hands;  

et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.  Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;
and the fourth reason is that the stone in women is located deeper than in men, which requires a deeper incision, and there is great risk involved. And if necessity demands it, you must seek a well-trained midwife, though she is rarely found, and if you cannot find one, then search for a discreet and virtuous female physician;  

et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;  
and provide her with wise counsel in women’s matters, or with a woman who knows some part of the art, and instruct her to do what you direct for the investigation of the stone;  

et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:  
and carefully observe whether the woman is a virgin:  

adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;  
in that case, she must insert her finger into the rectum and search for the stone;  

et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.  
and if she finds it, she must hold it under her finger, and you must instruct her to insert her finger into the patient’s vulva, search for the stone, and press firmly on the bladder with her left hand.  

S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;  
If she finds it, she must gradually move it from the entrance of the bladder downward until it reaches the root of the thigh;  

puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;  
then cut above the stone at the root of the thigh toward the middle of the vulva, where it has been moved and can be felt in that area;  

et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;  
and do not move her finger from above or below the stone, and make the incision small at first;  

puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:  
then insert the probe into the incision; if you feel the stone, enlarge the wound so the stone can come out, and know that there are many types of stones:  

c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.  
namely, small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and those with roots.  

si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.  
Thus, understand their forms to determine how they will exit.  

Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;  
And if the bleeding overwhelms you, apply powdered vitriol to the area and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops;  

puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;  
then return to your work until the stone is removed, and use the instruments I have described for extracting stones in men to assist you in your procedure;  

et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;  
and if the bleeding overwhelms you and comes from a cut artery, apply the powder to the area, compress it with tents and bandages, and do not continue; leave the stone and do not extract it, for the patient might die;  

puis cure la plaie.  
then treat the wound.  

Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.  
And when the heat from the blood has subsided and the area is no longer inflamed, return to your work until the stone is removed.  

de hernie carnouse  
About fleshy hernia  

Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;  
Watery hernia is nothing more than an accumulation of moisture or white syfac under the tissue of the testicles, which contains the egg;  

et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;  
and it is called "syfac," and sometimes it is precisely in the membrane of the egg, so one might think it is another egg;  

et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;  
and it is the membrane of the testicle between the white syfac we mentioned;  

et ceu n’avient se poc non.  
and this occurs only rarely.  

Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.  
And the formation of this hernia arises from weakness that affects the testicles, spreading this substance.  

Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:  
And sometimes it results from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors:  

ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;  
either a color resembling jaundice, or it is reddish blood, or black, or watery white, which happens most often;  

et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.  
and these are the signs to recognize this accumulation: if it is in the white syfac we mentioned, the abscess is round, slightly elongated like the shape of an egg, and the testicle is not visible, as it is surrounded by moisture.  

Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;  
And if the moisture is in the membrane itself, the abscess is round with a part of the egg visible, which makes one think it is another egg;  

et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;  
and if the moisture is between the membrane of the testicles and the white syfac, it can be felt clearly;  

donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.  
therefore, when you wish to know the color of the moisture, test it with the square introducer described earlier.  

Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.  
Based on what emerges after using the introducer, judge what is inside.  

Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;  
And when we treat it with surgery, the patient must first be bled as much as his strength and bodily fullness allow;  

puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;  
then recline him on his back on something slightly raised, and place many cloths beneath him;  

puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;  
then sit on his left, and instruct your assistant to sit on the right and stretch the penis toward one of the two sides of the testicle tissue;  

puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;  
then take the light spatula and cut the membrane of the testicles along its length to the root, making your incision straight, dividing the membrane of the testicles until you reach the white syfac, and peel it carefully as best as you can;  

puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;  
then pierce the syfac full of water with a wide opening, extract all the fluid, then apply your ointments, and stretch the syfac upward;  

et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;  
and do not touch the tissue of the testicles, only the syfac;  

cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;  
cut all of it or piece by piece, carefully removing it, for if you do not cut it thoroughly, the fluid will return;  

et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;  
and if the egg escapes during your procedure, return it to its place once you have completed the work on the syfac;  

puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then bring together the two edges of the testicle tissue with a single suture, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed.  

Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;  
And if you find the testicle corrupted by another disease, you must bind the vessels that are suspensory, fearing the flow of blood;  

puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.  
then cut the testicle along with the suspensory, and extract the testicle, and treat it as we have said.  

Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;  
And if fluid is gathered in two parts together, know that these are two branches;  

si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;  
then cut the other part just as you did the first one equally, then wipe the blood, and place in the wound wool soaked in rose oil;  

et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:  
and place outside other wool soaked in wine and oil, and place it over the two testicles, and put doubled cloths on top, and bind it all with a bandage in this manner:  

Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;  
Then take two cloths, and fill them with shredded wool in this form, and they should be joined by sewing at the waistband of the breeches, with one end reaching from the base to the back, and the other to the area of the thigh;  

et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;  
and the other two ends over the two groins, and all the compression should be gathered at the buckle of the breeches;  

et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;  
and sometimes this branch is treated with cautery instead of cutting with iron, and it is done by taking a fine knife-like cautery, and cutting the skin of the testicles, and heating it as we have said, so that the white sac containing the fluid is uncovered;  

si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:  
then take the cautery in this manner, and pierce that sac at the swollen areas, and scrape it with this fine heated cautery:  

Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;  
And cut it in every way you can, until you scrape everything out;  

et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;  
and ensure that the fire does not touch the testicle;  

et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;  
and know that this procedure is safer;  

et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;  
and you avoid the risk of blood flow, and it is gentler than the work of cutting;  

et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.  
and if anything opposes you, such as a hot abscess, blood flow, or anything else, treat what is opposing you according to what has been previously mentioned.  

Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;  
And if the patient is fearful and does not wish to endure this procedure because of its horror, then administer perforation, as I tell you, and when you are very certain by the signs we have described that the watery branch is there, make the patient sit on a raised seat;  

pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;  
then pierce the abscess at the lower part with the wide spatula, and make the perforation along the length of the body;  

et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;  
and the opening should be wide so that all the fluid may flow out;  

puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;  
then place cotton on the area, and bind it, and let it drain the remaining fluid, then treat it until the wound is healed;  

et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;  
and if the white tissue does not let the fluid exit through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to draw fluid from dropsical patients, the form of which was mentioned earlier;  

et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.  
and widen the wound a little, and know that the fluid will return, and will gather again after six months or so, and when it gathers as before, the patient will live out his days this way.  

de l’aposteme des coions  
Of the abscess of the testicles  

Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;  
Know that in the cutting of this branch there are dangers in many conditions, for which it seems to me that it is often better to leave it;  

et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.  
and I will tell you the procedure and the characteristics of the abscess.  

Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;  
I say therefore that many abscesses occur in the body, and especially in the testicles;  

et c’est par mout de cas.  
and it is from many causes.  

C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;  
It is namely from an excess of sharp and bitter fluid, which is spread to the testicles, or from trauma;  

et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;  
and the color of the abscess is like the color of the body;  

et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;  
and no pain is found, and the abscess is serious;  

et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.  
and sometimes there is a grave abscess, fearful and dangerous, and of dark color, and sometimes it comes from damage to an artery, or swelling of a vein.  

Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;  
When it is from damage to an artery, it is known by the disposition of the hot abscess, when you press it with your fingers;  

et ne covient mie que tu i touches.  
and you must not touch it.  

Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;  
The one caused by swelling of the vein is recognized by its reaction to the pressing of fingers, and it is possible to perform the incision on this condition and on the surrounding tissues;  

et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.  
and this involves cutting the heart of the testicles, then lifting the testicle upwards, extracting it from the white sac, and freeing the suspensory from all sides of the testicle.  

Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;  
If the testicle is already fused with its surrounding tissues, you must then extract the testicle and cut it;  

et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.  
and if it is adherent to the sac or to the vessels inside, you must free all this tissue and cut it in a rounded manner.  

Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.  
And if the growth of tissue is located at the rear, you must cut all of it and extract the testicle as we have described.  

Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  
And when your procedure is complete, fill the wound with wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.  

de l’aposteme des coions  
Of the abscess of the testicles  

Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;  
This is an abscess enclosed by a wrapping resembling a bud, accompanied by the softening of the testicles, and the patient moves with great difficulty when he walks;  

et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.  
and the treatment of this condition is nearly as fearsome as the one previously described, yet we will explain its procedure to you, according to what the ancients practiced.  

Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;  
The patient must sit on a raised seat, then you press down the suspensory of the testicles with your fingers, along with the vessels near the penis, and the assistant holds and stretches them tightly;  

puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;  
then cut across with the wide blade of the spatula at the level of the vessels until they are exposed, and then scrape from each side, as we have explained in the extraction of arteries in the temples;  

puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;  
then insert a needle with a double thread, and tie it at the first location where the swelling occurred, and tie it again at the other end;  

puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;  
then cut them in the middle straightly, along the length of the body, and remove the corrupted fluids;  

puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;
