then treat the wound as with the others where pus forms, ensuring that no vessel falls that nourishes one of the testicles;  

car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;  
for from this no harm comes, and if life reaches all the vessels, the testicles must be extracted along with all the vessels;  

si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.  
so that the organ does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and dries up and cannot recover.  

de la routure dou syfac  
Of the rupture of the sac  

Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;  
The occurrence of this branch is due to the rupture that occurs in the sac or the stretching over the abdomen in the groin area, which causes the intestines to descend through this rupture to one of the testicles;  

et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:  
and this rupture is either of the sac or of its stretching, and these two forms arise from many causes:  

ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;  
from trauma, or jumping, or straining, or lifting heavy loads, and similar causes;  

et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;  
and the signs when it is due to the stretching of the sac are that it happens little by little, over a long time, and does not occur suddenly;  

et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.  
and the abscess is uniform up to the base, because the sac presses against the intestine.  

Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.  
And the signs, when it is due to the rupture of the sac, are that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscess appears irregular, under the skin near the surface, due to the protrusion of the intestine and the body outside the sac.  

Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.  
And sometimes the mesentery descends along with the intestine and becomes trapped there, causing great pain for the patient, especially when it is pressed.  

Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.  
And in these treatments, there is fear of using iron, which is why it must be avoided. 

Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;  
And the method of the operation is that you instruct the patient to push the intestine back inside the wound with his hand, if he can do so;  

puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;  
then hold his neck between your hands and raise his thighs;  

puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;  
then stretch the skin above and cut along the entire length of the skin of the testicles;  

puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;  
then insert the edges of the incision with hooks as needed to open the wound, and ensure they are positioned so the bone can be exposed;  

puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;  
then peel back the fascia that is beneath the skin of the testicles until the white hard fascia is uncovered on all sides;  

puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;  
then insert your index finger into the area surrounding the testicle, between the white fascia beneath the skin of the egg and the second fascia, and separate the part behind the egg and between the second fascia;  

et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;  
and then move the testicle with your right hand inside the skin of the testicles, stretching the white fascia upward with your left hand, and lift the egg along with the fascia toward the incision;  

et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;  
and instruct the assistant to stretch the egg upward, and untie what is behind the binding;  

et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;  
and check with your fingers if any intestine is entangled with the white hard fascia, and if you find anything, push it back into the abdomen;  

puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;  
then take a needle with a thick thread made of ten strands, and insert it into the back part of the fascia, which is after the skin of the testicles;  

aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;  
after the incision, then cut the ends of the threads that are visible, so that there are four threads left;  

puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;  
then gather them one over the other in the form of a cross, and tie the fascia, which we mentioned is beneath the skin of the testicles, with a strong binding from two sides;  

puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;  
then wrap the ends of the threads and tie them tightly on both sides, so that none of the vessels nourishing them can enter, preventing the formation of a hot abscess;  

et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;  
and then place another binding over the first one, two finger-widths from it, and after these two bindings leave from the fascia beneath the skin of the testicles the width of one finger;  

et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;  
and after that, follow the roundness of the structure that the egg forms;  

puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;  
then cut in the area beneath the skin of the testicles, until the blood flows, as we mentioned before;  

puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.  
then apply wool soaked in oil, place it in the wound, and use the binding that we described.  

Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.  
And sometimes the white fascia we mentioned is cauterized after the incision, to prevent the risk of blood leakage.  

Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;  
For this happens often, and leave the binding in place until it falls off on its own;  

et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;  
and if it delays falling off, sprinkle it with warm water and apply what we described until it falls off;  

puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.  
then treat the wound with further care until it is fully healed.  

de hernie carnouse  
On fleshy hernia  

En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.  
In this type of rupture, I have never seen anyone who dared to perform the treatment with iron.  

Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;  
And the ancients said it is treated like the rupture that surrounds the life force, in such a way that you tie the vessels after the incision just beneath them;  

puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;  
then cut through it and treat the abscess of what is active until the vessels are detached;  

et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and treat it as we have described until it is healed.  

Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;  
Sometimes a rupture occurs in the groin, as we have said, and the location opens;  

et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;  
and none of the intestines descend into the testicles, and if any do descend, it is little, and they return by themselves every time;  

et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;  
and yet, if it remains too long in this state, the wound or fascia grows until the intestines descend;  

et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;  
and this happens due to the stretching of the fascia in the groin, as we said, for it becomes stretched, then softened and swollen, and the location opens;  

et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;  
and the treatment is by cauterization, as we have said before;  

et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:  
and sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:  

et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;  
and it is that the patient lies often on his back between your hands, then you cut the location of the swollen rupture wide, according to the size of three fingers;  

et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;  
and then pull out the fascia beneath the skin that follows, then take the bandage and place it over the visible location of the fascia;  

et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;  
and press it deep into the abdomen, then sew the two visible locations of the fascia above the end of the bandage, and sew both;  

puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;  
then remove the end of the bandage, and do not cut the fascia nor stretch the egg or anything else, as I informed you in the treatment of the rupture of the intestines;  

puis le cure par la cure des plaies.  
then treat it as you would treat wounds.  

Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.  
And when you cut the threads, cleanse it and treat the wound until it is healed.  

Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.  
The fascia is restricted and does not protrude in the rupture, and cauterization is better in this location and closer to recovery.  

de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions  
On the softening of the skin of the testicles  

Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;  
Many times, the skin of the testicles softens in some men because the flesh inside is softened, and it is unsightly to behold;  

et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;  
and it is necessary, when one wants to treat it, to make the patient lie on his back and cut the softened skin over the natural skin;  

puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;  
then join the two edges with a seam, and if you wish, first sew the excess of the softened skin with three or four firm stitches;  

puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.  
then cut between the stitches, and treat it as you would other wounds, until it is healed and the threads fall out.  

dou chastrement  
On castration  

Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;  
Know that castration is forbidden in our law, and for this reason, I would prefer not to speak of it in this book;  

et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:  
and it is only necessary for two purposes:  

dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;  
one is that the physician knows how to answer when asked about it, and knows the treatment;  

et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.  
and the other, because we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as goats, sheep, cats, and other animals.  

Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:  
I say then that castration is done in two ways:  

ou par atraction, ou par fendure.  
either by pulling or by cutting.  

En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;  
In the method done by pulling, we make the animal sit in warm water until the testicles are softened and hang loose;  

puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.  
then take them in your hand until they are retracted and you no longer feel them.  

Du chastrement de taille:  
On castration by cutting:  

covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;  
you must hold the animal and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory cord and cut over each egg with one stroke, after you have carefully skinned them;  

et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;  
and leave a small part of the fascia and the thin fascia covering the vessels;  

et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;  
and this method of castration is better than the one done by pulling, because with pulling, part of the testicles may remain, causing the animal to desire lust;  

puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.  
then treat the wound until it is healed.  

des hermofrodites  
On hermaphrodites  

Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:  
Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways in men:  

l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.  
one is when between the two testicles appears something resembling the form of a woman’s nature, with hair, and sometimes urine flows from it.  

Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.  
And the other form is in women, where on the pubic region there is something resembling a penis and two testicles.  

Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;  
And the treatment for both the man and the woman is to cut away all the additional flesh and treat it as you would other wounds;  

en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.  
in the second form, where urine leaks through the skin of the testicles in men, there is no cure.  

de la tentigene  
Of the tentigene  

Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;  
Tentigene is flesh added to the natural part, such that it is very unsightly to see;  

et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.  
and some women have it as large as a hand, and this is the cure.  

Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;  
You must grasp the excess of the tentigene with your hand or hooks, and cut it gently;  

et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;  
and not go too deep, so that no flow of blood occurs there, then treat it with another remedy until it is healed;  

et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».  
and for another flesh that grows at the mouth of the womb, and fills it, and sometimes erupts out, and resembles a cow’s udder, and for this the ancients called it the “cow disease.”  

Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.  
You must cut it, as we have said of the tentigene, and treat it until it is healed.  

de erratique  
Of erratique  

Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;  
Erratique is when the nature of the woman is not pierced, or the opening is small;  

et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;  
and it is natural from birth, or occurs due to illness that has come there;  

ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;  
or it is by added flesh, or by a thin or thick syfac, and it is formed deep in the womb, or on the sides, or beneath, or wherever it may be;  

et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;  
and it prevents conception and childbirth, and perhaps also the menstruation;  

et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.  
and the recognition of this is through examination by the caretaker.  

Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.  
If the obstruction is close and visible, feel for it with your fingers or a probe.  

S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:  
If it is a thin syfac, and it is close to the two lips, hasten and break it thus:  

met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;  
place your two index fingers together, and let the woman lie on her back, with her legs spread apart;  

puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;  
then stretch the two lips firmly, until the thin syfac is broken and the obstruction is opened;  

puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.  
then take wool, soak it in oil, and place it on the spot, and let the woman lie with a man each day, so it cannot close up.  

Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.  
And if the syfac is hard and thick, you must cut it with a spatula-like tool resembling a myrtle leaf.  

Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;  
If the obstruction is of grown flesh, suspend it with a hook and cut it;  

et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;  
and use medicines to staunch the blood, such as acacia, dragon’s blood, frankincense, mixed with egg white;  

puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;  
then insert a wide lead cane, so that the wound cannot close up;  

et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;  
and keep it so for a long time, and insert a tent of dry linen;  

puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.  

Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.  
And when in the womb grown flesh appears, it must be cut in this manner, unless it is a cancerous ulcer.  

Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.  
For a cancerous ulcer in the womb, one must not touch it with iron.  

des emorroides  
Of hemorrhoids  

Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;  
Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood frequently flows, and when hemorrhoids are old, they become thelul.  

et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.  
And we have already described in the division their appearances and signs, and I will now discuss those that receive treatment.  

Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.  
I say that hemorrhoids and thelul, when they are deep in the womb and are not perceptible to touch, are not treated with iron.  

Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.  
Those that are at the mouth of the womb, which can be felt, are those that can be treated.  

Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;  
It is necessary then to place the woman in a cool room, then grasp the thelul with forceps, and cut it at its roots, then sprinkle medicines to staunch the blood, such as acacia, dragon’s blood, frankincense, and similar substances;  

puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;  
then press her feet against the wall for an hour, and then place her in cold water;  

et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.  
and if a flow of blood occurs, have her sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate peel, galls, and similar things, and then take barley flour, mix it with honey and vinegar, and make a poultice to place on her back.  

Et se il estainche, c’est boin.  
And if it staunches, it is good.  

Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;  
If not, then apply cupping glasses to her back and breasts without cutting.  

puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.  
Then take wool, soak it in the juice of plantain or dog rose with old wine, and apply it to the area.  

Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;  
And when the swelling subsides, treat the area with ointment until it is healed.  

et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;  
And the one called "albathir" is red and resembles a rough surface, and it must be cut as I have said of the thelul;  

et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and then treat it until it is healed.  

des apostemes de la marris  
Of ulcers of the womb  

Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.  
Many types of ulcers appear in the womb, such as cancer, stony ulcers, herpes, estiomenes, fistulas, hemorrhoids, hot ulcers, and many other conditions that I have mentioned in the division.  

Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;  
It is necessary then that I speak in this treatise of the hot ulcer that occurs in the womb, which is not one of those ulcers that collects pus;  

et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.  
and if you wish to know the work of iron, see if the ulcer is acute in the beginning of its appearance, full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red when you can see it.  

Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;  
Then do not hasten to pierce it, but allow it to mature until the pain subsides;  

et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;  
and then have the patient sit on a seat, and place two small stools for support, leaning on her back and bringing her feet to the outer sides of the legs;  

et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;  
and her thighs should be spread, and her arms placed under her knees, and bind them well with a good tie;  

puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;  
then position her body toward the right side, and administer the instrument used to open the mouth of the womb, of which the form is described hereafter;  

et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;  
and it is necessary that when you wish to use this instrument, you first insert a probe to determine the depth of the womb, so that what enters from the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and does not injure the patient;  

et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;  
and if the instrument is too large, you must cover the depth of the womb with cloths, so that the instrument does not cause harm.  

et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.  
And you must place the horn of the instrument on top, and hold the instrument.  

Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;  
And when the ulcer opens, and it is soft to the touch, you must cut it at the top with a sharp spatula.  

et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;  
And when the pus is emptied, you must place tents soaked in rose oil or dry green oil in the wound.  

et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;  
And place the tent from the wound to the depth of the womb, and apply clean wool soaked in water or mallow decoction over the womb and the wound.  

puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;  
Then treat it after two days with suitable ointments until it is healed.  

et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;  
And sometimes the womb and the wound are washed with an enema of water and honey, and then water with cooked roots of lily and long aristolochia.  

puis reveigne a l’oignement.  
Then return to the ointment.  

Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.  
And if the wound has spread into the womb, it is necessary that you avoid cauterizing with iron, but treat it as we have explained in the section.  

de l’enfantement  
Of childbirth  

Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:  
It is first necessary for the midwife to know the pattern of natural childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman pressing downward and desiring to breathe the air.  

adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;  
Then the child hastens to come out.  

adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;  
Then know that this childbirth is in the natural form, and the emergence is with its head, and the afterbirth with it.  

et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;  
And when you see these signs, you must press lightly on her belly so that the child comes out quickly.  

car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;  
For when it descends with its head, the afterbirth comes out with it, and the womb is cleansed of its excess by proper purification.  

et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.  
And the one that comes otherwise does not come naturally.  

Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;  
For it sometimes comes feet first, or the body or head appears, or the hands, or it comes on its belly or sideways, and is sometimes turned on its neck, and in other bad positions.  

si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.  
Thus, the midwife must be wise and skillful in these matters, and guard herself against errors and deceptions, and I will show you all the positions and how to help them.  

Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;  
If the child comes headfirst in a natural birth, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and her strength is weak, have her sit on a seat, or have women hold her.  

et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:  
And anoint her genital area with oil or cooked fenugreek, and then the midwife inserts between her fingers the small spatumile described here.  

et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;  
And split the afterbirth, and cut it with her nail so that the moisture within runs out.  

et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;  
And press the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, it is necessary to administer an enema with fenugreek mucilage and sesame oil.  

puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:  
Then make her inhale and sneeze with spices, and hold her mouth and nose for a moment.  

si istra maintenant l’enfes.  
The child will now come out.  

Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;  
And if both hands come out first, you must gently push them back, little by little.  

et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;  
And if they cannot be pushed back, place the woman on a seat and lift her feet high.  

puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;  
Then tilt the seat to the ground, and hold the woman so that she does not fall during the tilting.  

et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.  
And if the hands cannot enter, and the child dies, cut its hands with the knife previously mentioned, and extract the child, and adjust it properly.  

de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés  
On the delivery of the child feet first  

Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;  
When the child comes feet first, you must push it upward.  

et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;  
And then turn it little by little until it is aligned.  

puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.  
Then take one of its feet and extend it little by little.  

Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;  
When it moves up to the thighs, instruct her to push and make her sneeze with spices.  

si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.  
Then it will come out if God wills it.  

Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.  
And if it does not emerge as we have said, turn it little by little until it is in the natural position.  

Car adonques ist il legierement.  
For then it will come out easily.  

Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;  
And if it does not come out as we have said, take mallow mucilage, sesame oil, and melted gum, and grind them all in a mortar.  

et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;  
And apply this ointment to the woman’s genital area inside and out, then make her sit in warm water up to below her ribs.  

et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;  
And when she is softened below, make a suppository of myrrh, place it inside her, and leave it for an hour.  

puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.  
Then make her sit on a seat, then make her sneeze, close her mouth and nose, and lightly press her belly, for the child will now emerge.  

de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous  
On the delivery of the child knee-first  

Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;  
When the child comes in this position, the midwife should insert her hands little by little.  

puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;  
Then it should be turned over its neck, with its feet hanging downward, and the woman lying on a bed.  

et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;  
And fold its hands little by little, then place her hands on her belly, and remove the cushions below her until she is positioned downward.  

et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;  
And if the child does not emerge, take its feet and move them firmly, then move the belly upward, then insert your hands.  

et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;  
And draw the child out little by little.  

et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.  
And instruct the woman to push until the child comes out.  

de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant  
On the delivery of the child with one arm extended  

I covient engignier a ramener la main:  
It is necessary to manipulate to bring the arm back.  

s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;  
If it cannot be brought back, make the woman stand up and walk.  

s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;  
If she cannot walk, make her lie on a bed and spread her legs firmly.  

puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;  
Then administer the mucilage I have described.  

et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;  
And if she does not give birth, make her sit on a seat, then work to bring the arm back.  

et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.  
And draw the child out in the natural position, make her sneeze, and instruct her to push until the child comes out.  

de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere  
On the delivery of the child with its head back, hands spread, and face turned toward its mother’s back  

I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;  
The midwife must hold it with her hand, then turn it little by little and guide it gently.  

et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;  
And when it is aligned, apply mallow mucilage and oil to the genital area, as we have said, then instruct her to move little by little.  

et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;  
And when you have done this, make her sit on a seat and instruct her to push.  

et la fai esternuer.  
And make her sneeze.  

de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine  
On this same procedure with the afterbirth  

Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;  
When it comes out in this manner with the afterbirth, cut the afterbirth with your nail so that the moisture is drained.  

et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;  
And if the child is hanging by its face and neck, cut it from the cord so that it is not retained, and the child does not die.  

puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:  
Then push the child inside until you have positioned it as it should be, and instruct the woman to push again.  

adonques si istra legierement.  
Then it will come out easily.  

de l’issue des gemelz  
On the delivery of twins  

Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;  
Know that twins are often born, and sometimes three or four are born.  

et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.  
And this is not a strange thing, though it happens rarely.  

Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;  
Two [children] are a strange thing, and they rarely live.  

je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;  
I know this, that they are multiplied and separated by the membrane that divides them, which is attached to the cord.  

et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.  
And sometimes they emerge as naturally as one alone, as we have said.  

Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;  
And if they emerge with difficulty, treat them as we have explained, and let the midwife be skillful and act quickly and gently.  

et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.  
And let her act in such a way as to bring them safely to health.  

de plusors enfans  
On multiple children  

Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;  
Sometimes one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, or more up to fifteen are formed in the womb, and they are all shaped in the form of children by the design of the glorious Creator. It is necessary for the midwife to know all this, for such things may happen unexpectedly.  

si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.  
Let her act accordingly as required.  

de l’enfant mort  
Of the dead child  

Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;  
When you treat the woman of the dead child or womb, as I have said in the section, and it does not come out, and you are forced to operate with your hands;  

si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;  
it is necessary that you know if the woman is of sound health, and does not have a condition where she fears death;  

si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;  
it is necessary that the woman be laid on her back, with her head inclined downward, and her legs raised;  

et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;  
and the assistant holds her from both sides, or she is tied to the bed so that she is not moved by the descent of the child;  

puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;  
then rub the mouth of the womb with moist oils mixed with mallow mucilage, fenugreek, and flaxseed, and then anoint the attendant's hands with these oils and mucilages;  

puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;  
then insert them into the womb gently, then find a place where the instruments should be placed, and check if the child is positioned to descend head first;  

si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;  
if so, insert the instruments into its eyes or neck or mouth or palate or under the chin or in the joint or near the ribs, and if the descent is feet first, insert them at the ankles and the lower ribs;  

et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;  
and it is necessary that the instrument be held in the right hand, and the curve placed between the fingers of the left hand, and insert it with the whole hand gently, and fix the instrument in one of the places we have mentioned, until it reaches the hollow part;  

et c’est li forme de l’oncine:  
and this is the shape of the instrument:  

puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;  
then insert another instrument opposite, or a third if needed, so that the extraction is balanced;  

et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:  
and then extend it evenly, moving from one side to the other, to allow the remains to come out, and the instruments should have teeth to hold the remains, as shown here in the design:  

Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;  
And if a part remains, the attendant should anoint one of their fingers with oil, insert it into that part, and pull the remaining part;  

et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.  
and if none remains, then place the instrument at a higher location, and do this until everything comes out completely.  

Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;  
And if one hand comes forward before the other, and it cannot be pulled back due to constriction, you must wrap it in a cloth until it fully emerges;  

puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.  
then cut it at the joint of the palm or the wrist, and similarly you must do the same for the other hand and for both feet.  

Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;  
And if the child’s head is large and narrow at the exit, or if fluid has accumulated in the head, you must insert the spiked spatula between your fingers, split the head, and extract the fluid;  

ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;  
or you break it with the instrument called "almidach," the design of which is provided with the instruments in the chapter following this one;  

et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;  
and do the same if the child has a naturally large head;  

et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;  
and then pull out the bones with forceps, and if the head escapes but is stuck in the joint, it must be split so that the fluids from the chest come out;  

et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;  
and if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces as much as you can;  

et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.  
and if it is swollen in the abdomen or under the ribs, you must pierce it until the fluids flow.  

Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.  
And if the child is on its feet, the extraction is easy, and guiding it to the mouth of the womb is simple.  

Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;  
And if it is narrow in the abdomen or the chest, you must extract it with a cloth wrapped around your hand;  

et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;  
and cut the abdomen or the chest until the fluids within flow;  

et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;  
and if the other members are removed and the head remains, the attendant should place their hand deep into the womb and pull it to the mouth of the womb;  

puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;  
then insert one or two instruments and extract it;  

et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;  
and if the mouth of the womb is constricted due to a hot abscess that has formed there, no work should be done on it, but rather moist and fatty substances should be applied;  

et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.  
and apply poultices and wash with softening and moistening waters.  

Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;  
And if the child is on its side and you can reposition it, apply what we have said about a living child;  

et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.  
and if that is not possible, then extract it piece by piece, leaving nothing of the afterbirth.  

Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;  
And once you have done this, apply what we have said for hot abscesses that occur in the womb;  

et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.  
and if there is a flow of blood, it should be treated with astringent water, and other remedies should be applied.  

Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.  
And I saw a woman in whose womb a child had died, then another was conceived on top of it, and the other also died.  

Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.  
After a long time, an abscess formed in the groin, swelled so much that it opened, and began to emit a great stench.  

je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.  
I was called to treat it, and I thought for a long time, but I could not close the wound.  

Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.  
I applied a strong drawing poultice, and a bone came out, and after a few days, others followed.  

Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.  
I marveled greatly, because the womb has no bones.  

Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.  
Then I thought they were the bones of a dead child.  

Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;  
I probed the wound and extracted many bones until the woman was in a better condition;  

et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;  
and the woman lived a long time this way, with a little discharge continually coming from the place;  

et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.  
and I have recalled this chapter only to say that when the practitioner encounters a strange situation, they must know how to provide help.  

dou ramener la marris a son leu  
On returning the womb to its place  

Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;  
Here follows the shape of the press by which the books are lifted;  

et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.  
and with two screws at the two ends of the two straps.  

Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;  
However, the horns should be finer than the restrainer and should be made of ebony or boxwood;  

et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;  
and the opening of the wood should be one finger wide, the edge of the wood one finger wide, and one and a half palms in length;  

et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;  
and in the middle of the two straps there should be two additions of the same wood, securely fixed at either end, half a palm in length or slightly more;  

et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.  
and these two additions are inserted into the mouth of the womb to open it when the two horns are turned.  

Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;  
Another form, similar but finer and lighter, should be made of ebony or boxwood, resembling forceps;  

et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;  
and it should have two additions at its two ends, as you see, one palm in length and two fingers wide;  

et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;  
and when you want to open the womb with the instrument, have the woman sit on a bed, with her feet dangling and her legs spread, then insert the two joined additions into the womb, and hold the head of the instrument below between her thighs;  

puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.  
then operate the instrument with your hand, as you would with forceps, according to the amount you want to open the mouth of the womb, until the assistant accomplishes what they intend.  

Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;  
These instruments are all superior, and their designs are numerous;  

et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.  
and when the surgeon has prepared them, the work is much faster and more efficient for their purpose.  

Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.  
Do not neglect the instrument; ensure it is ready, as its necessity cannot be excused.  

Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;  
When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, then make her sneeze with the appropriate method, and press your hands on her mouth and nose;  

et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.  
and if it comes out this way, all is well.  

Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;  
If not, take a pot, make a hole in its lid, and put in herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia wood, and centaury.  

toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;  
All these herbs, or some of them, should be boiled in water in the pot over the fire.  

puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;  
Then place a tube in the hole of the pot, with the other end in the mouth of the womb, and hold it there until the vapor enters the womb.  

puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.  
Then make her sneeze, as we have said.  

Si saut li secondine hastanment.  
The afterbirth will quickly emerge.  

Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;  
And if it remains after this treatment and does not come out, instruct the midwife to moisten her left hand with sesame oil or marshmallow mucilage, then insert it into the womb and search for the afterbirth.  

et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;  
When she finds it, she should take it and stretch it little by little straight out so that the womb does not collapse during the extraction.  

mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;  
But she must move it lightly to the right and left, then pull it.  

si venra et se desaerdra.  
It will come out and detach.  

Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;  
And if the mouth of the womb is already constricted, we have spoken of the treatment of sneezing and the fumigation with herbs.  

et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;  
And if it does not come out with all that we have described, be careful not to pull recklessly.  

mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;  
Rather, you must tie what is at the mouth of the womb to the woman’s thigh, then administer a clyster with tetrapharmacon ointment.  

si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;  
This will soften it, reposition it, and make it come out.  

mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.  
But still, when it softens, a foul odor may arise, affecting the stomach and head, harming the patient.  

Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:  
Thus, suitable fumigations are necessary for this.  

aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.  
Some of the ancients recommended fumigating with watercress and dried figs.  

Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:  
The design of the instrument used to fumigate the woman for retained blood or afterbirth is this:  

Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;  
It is made of glass, resembling a tube, with the narrow end placed in the womb and the wide end above the fire.  

et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.  
The fumigation should be over embers and held there until it is used up, then another should be prepared.  

de percier lou fondement  
On piercing the anus  

Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:  
Many children are born with an anus that is not pierced, instead blocked by a thin membrane.  

si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;  
Thus, the midwife must pierce that membrane with her finger, not with a sharp blade, and ensure the sphincter is not harmed.  

puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.  
Then place wool soaked in wine and oil on it, and apply ointments until it is healed.  

Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.  
If you fear it will close again, insert a lead tube into the opening and leave it for several days, removing it when the child needs to pass waste.  

Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;  
Sometimes this obstruction comes from the closure of a wound or abscess.  

si covient coper celui soudement:  
Then the closure must be cut.  

si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.  
Treat it as we have described with the lead tube.  

de la fistule dou fondement  
On fistulas of the anus  

Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;  
Fistulas that appear below the anus are swellings and enlargements near or between the two parts of the anus, sometimes singular or multiple.  

et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;  
When this swelling becomes old, it opens and discharges white watery moisture or subtle pus, and sometimes these fistulas are perforating.  

et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.  
They are identified by the fact that stool or gas escapes through them when the patient defecates, and sometimes a worm emerges.  

Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;  
Some fistulas pierce as far as the bladder or halfway up the penis.  

et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.  
They can extend to the junction of the thigh or even to the tailbone.  

Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:  
Thus, one recognizes a perforating fistula of the anus and a non-perforating one.  

et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.  
This is done by inserting your index finger into the anus and a fine bronze or iron needle into the fistula if it is not twisted.  

Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;  
If it is twisted, insert a thin lead probe or a horsehair until you can feel it with your finger.  

et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:  
If you cannot feel it and no stool, gas, or worm comes from the opening as we described:  

saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;  
Know that it does not perforate.  

si te haste dou curer.  
Then proceed to treat it quickly.  

Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.  
And when the fistula perforates to the bladder or the urinary canal, urine leaks from it and cannot be healed with medicines.  

S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;  
If it perforates to the junction of the thigh, the probe will reach that location.  

s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;  
If there is no twisting and the surrounding area is painful, pus will constantly flow from it, and neither medicines nor healing ointments will help.  

et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.  
For these perforating fistulas, there is no cure except through surgery, despite the vain attempts of foolish physicians who meddle with them.  

En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;  
For a fistula that is not perforating and not old, there is hope for healing with surgery, as I have experienced. The patient should lie on their back under your hands.  

et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;  
Lift their legs over their thighs, and their thighs should be inclined towards their abdomen.  

puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.  
Then insert a bronze probe, or a lead one if there is twisting, until you determine where the probe reaches.  

Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;  
If the patient feels it around the anus, you must insert your index finger and confirm if the probe has perforated it.  

et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;  
And if you feel with your finger a membrane or flesh, then you know it is perforating.  

si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.  
Do not attempt to treat it, as it cannot be healed.  

On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;  
It is said that some can indeed be healed, but this rarely happens.  

et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;  
The method of aid involves heating a fine cautery to match the width of the fistula, as previously described.  

et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;  
Insert it while hot into the fistula until it reaches near the anus.  

et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;  
Do this two or three times until you are sure the damaged tissues, resembling the quill of a bird, are burned away.  

et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.  
Then treat it with probes moistened with butter until the burnt tissue comes out, followed by healing ointments to regenerate and close the flesh.  

S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.  
If it heals this way, that is good.  

Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;  
If not, it cannot be healed in any other way.  

et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;  
If the probe enters but does not reach the finger placed in the anus, and there is a thick covering of flesh or membrane between your finger and the probe, examine the fistula where this covering leads.  

si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;  
Cut at the start of the fistula, continually insert the probe further, and follow with the cautery until it reaches the end of the probe.  

et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;  
The probe will be freed and fall out.  

puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.  
Then clean out the damaged tissues, which resemble a bird’s quill, leaving none behind.  

Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.  
If blood overcomes you and interferes with your work, cauterize it with fire or a sharp medicine.  

Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:  
For a fire cautery achieves two good results:  

c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;  
namely, the burning away of damaged tissues and the stopping of bleeding and moisture.  

puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;  
Then treat it with probes moistened with butter or crushed substances until the site expels pus and the burnt tissue is removed in it.  

puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.  
Then heal the wound with closing ointments that generate firm flesh, using dry medicines.  

Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.  
For once it is restored, it is healed and does not return.  

Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.  
If the fistula reaches deep into the anus and is distant from the body, insert your finger into the anus and investigate this.  

Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:  
If you feel the probe and there is tissue, membrane, or flesh between them, or it is close to perforating, then proceed with confidence and hope using one of three methods:  

ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;  
either cauterize it as described, cut it down to its depth, or if possible, insert probes and treat it as before.  

et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;  
Do not go too deep, lest you cut the structure that holds the anus, causing involuntary stool leakage.  

puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;  
Then treat it as we have described.  

par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;  
Perhaps it will be healed, or you can remove the covering and clean it once it is cut near the anus, either with a probe or another sharp instrument.  

puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;  
Then clean the damaged tissue in the wound as thoroughly as you can.  

puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:  
Next, work to restore the wound and ensure the fistula remains in the area away from the anus.  

si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.  
This will be easier for the patient.  

Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:  
And sometimes fistulas are treated in this manner:  

et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:  
and it is when you insert the tent into the fistula, and it is at the side of the anus near the skin above, then take a tent pierced at the tip in this shape:  

Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.  
And insert a twisted thread into it, and insert the tent with the thread into the fistula until it reaches the tip.  

S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;  
If it pierces into the margin of the anus inside, then draw the thread from that opening, so that you place your finger in the anus;  

et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;  
and pull the end of the thread, and join the two ends together, and tighten one against the other, and leave it for one or two days;  

et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;  
and tighten it occasionally until the thread cuts the flesh between the two, and they fall away;  

puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.  
then treat the wound until it is healed and healthy.  

Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.  
If the fistula does not pierce through, make it pierce in all the ways you can, unless it is too deep.  

Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
For it is not appropriate to use the ligature to cut so deeply, and then treat it, as we have said, until it is healed.  

Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;  
The shape of the sharp spatula used to open the fistula is very pointed on one side and cutting;  

et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:  
and not on the other side, so that one does not cut what should not be cut, as you see here:  

des emorroydes  
Of hemorrhoids  

Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:  
Hemorrhoids are of two kinds:  

ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;  
either they are inside the anus, like grains of grape, and there are small and large ones, and they often bleed, and there is one or more, and they are outside the anus and at the rim of the anus;  

mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;  
but those that are outside have little moisture, and often leak a little yellowish fluid or a little blood, and have the color of the body;  

et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;  
and the treatment for those inside the anus is to instruct the patient to strain when going to the bathroom, so that the hemorrhoids protrude, and the threads become visible;  

si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;  
then act quickly, and seize it with pincers, or hold it with your fingernail, then cut it at its roots;  

et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;  
and if the pincers cannot hold them because of their moisture, take a small cloth, or cotton, or a piece of camel-hair fabric;  

et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;  
and extract them with your fingers, then cut them, and sprinkle on some hot powders to act as a cauterizing agent;  

ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;  
or cauterize them as described in the chapter on cauterization, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed;  

et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;  
and if the hemorrhoids cannot protrude, give the patient a sharp and biting enema to wash what is in the anus, so that they may protrude clearly;  

cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;  
when the patient strains, and the hemorrhoids are outside the anus, the treatment is simple;  

et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.  
it is to grasp them with your fingernail or pincers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and fear the use of a blade.  

Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:  
Then you must perform the suturing in this manner:  

pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;  
take a twisted thread, and thread it into a needle, then draw the thread above and pierce the needle on the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread below the needle, and make it wide;  

et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;  
and tighten the thread firmly, then tie the thread, and withdraw the needle, and do the same with all the others, and leave one to drain the excess blood;  

puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;  
then place on the anus a cloth moistened with rose oil or wax, and apply it to the anus, and instruct the patient to rest;  

et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
and then leave it until they fall away, and when they have fallen, treat them with ointments and other remedies until they are healed.  

dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement  
Of the drying up of stool or the anus  

Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.  
Many times stool dries up in the intestine, and from the constriction of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine is ineffective.  

Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;  
Then you must scrape at the surface with the tip of a spatula or your fingernail to remove the crust above, which prevents moisture;  

puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;  
then treat it until it is healed as is necessary;  

et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;  
and if it cannot heal, begin the scraping again more forcefully than before, until it bleeds greatly and is flayed;  

puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.  
then treat it until it is healed.  

dou fremit  
Of fremitus  

Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;  
Formice is a small false growth around the body, and it goes very deep;  

et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.  
and sometimes it is caused by cold, and it feels like a dead fremitus, and it appears all over the body, more in the hands than elsewhere.  

Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;  
And the treatment is to take the quill of a goose feather, or a strong feather from a vulture, and place that quill over the fremitus, so that the circle surrounds the fremitus completely;  

puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.  
then turn your hand with the quill until you cut all around the fremitus, and push it deeply, and scrape the fremitus from its roots.  

Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:  
And if you wish, do this with a bronze or iron quill shaped in this way, being precise below and pulling above:  

ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.  
not piercing, for better grip with the finger and better pressure.  

Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.  
And if you wish, cauterize the fremitus as explained earlier in the chapter on cauterization.  

de la forme dou clistere  
Of the form of the enema  

Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;  
Sometimes enemas are made from silver, brass, molten bronze, or hammered bronze;  

et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.  
and sometimes these instruments are made small or large, according to those for whom they are prepared.  

Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.  
Thus, those used in the treatment of children and the weak or delicate are small.  

Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:  
The shape of both small and large enemas is wide above, where the chamber is fastened, as follows:  

et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;  
and it should have a separation where the chamber is fastened, as you see, and the end should be pierced inside;  

et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;  
and it should have two openings on one side, and one on the other;  

et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;
