Then extend the finger and push the dislocation as far as you can until it returns, then support the head of the finger and stretch it toward the part where it is disjointed.  

et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;  
And leave it for two days, then set it straight that day.  

et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;  
And at night bind it, as we have said, and during the day unbind it, make it move, and rebind it at night.  

et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;  
And do this often until it becomes firm, and do the same if it is dislocated to the front of the hand, and proceed as you did earlier, until it is healed.  

et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.  
And do the same when it is dislocated to another side.  

dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos  
Of the dislocation of the spine of the back  

Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.  
When the spine of the back or neck is dislocated, or there are several dislocations, there is no treatment, for death hastens the patient's end.  

Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.  
And the signs are that excretions escape without will, and they cannot control them, and often some limb is paralyzed, either both thighs or both arms or one.  

Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;  
And often the spine moves in four directions.  

celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:  
The one that moves backward is called "gibosity."  

li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:  
The treatment is to consider if the gibosity has been present since childhood.  

si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.  
Then there is no treatment or healing at all.  

Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;  
And the one that comes from falling or blows or similar causes, the ancients spoke of treatments with elaborate explanations, though not all are very effective.  

mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.  
But I have summarized it according to my understanding and have designed instruments in various ways.  

Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;  
I say that in the gibosity that appears at the front of the chest, there is neither remedy nor cure.  

et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;  
And likewise for the one that appears directly on both sides, no cure is possible except specifically for the one at the back, as I have said.  

et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;  
And it is that the patient should be stretched face down on a flat surface and have straw underneath them so they do not injure themselves.  

puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;  
Then drive one stake firmly into the ground at the head and another at the feet, and tie one strap under the patient’s armpits and another at the hips, knees, and ankles.  

et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;  
And two assistants should pull the straps, one at the head and the other at the feet, through the two stakes.  

et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.  
And the stakes should be well secured as we have described, and the doctor should press their palms firmly on the spine until it returns to place.  

Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;  
And if it does not return through this treatment, take a plank three cubits long, with one end against the wall, and have the patient lie on their side, placing the head of the plank against the wall, then the middle of the plank over the spine.  

et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;  
And the doctor should place their feet on the other end of the plank and press firmly until it returns to its place.  

et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.  
And if you wish, do this using a winch that turns by hand.  

Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;  
And you must drive two stakes at the head of the patient, one cubit apart, and two more near the feet, with a space of one palm’s width between each stake above and below.  

et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;  
And each stake should have a hole through which the winch passes, and the stakes must be firmly set in the ground so they do not move.  

et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;  
And between each pair of stakes, there should be a rotating stake around which the straps turn, and the two rotating stakes should have two small pegs, each a palm long, to turn the winch.  

et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.  
Then tie the strap under the armpits to the winch at the head and the other strap at the feet to the winch there, and each assistant should turn their winch along with the strap, while the doctor aligns the spine as we have described.  

Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;  
And when it is aligned, apply a drying plaster with plenty of egg, then lint, and then a splint made of a small plank three fingers long, which covers the site of the gibosity and the healthy part of the vertebra, then bind it with a strap as we have described, and the patient should use delicate nourishment until they are healed.  

et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;  
And if anything arises at the end of the healing, administer softening and soothing medicines along with the splint we mentioned earlier.  

et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;  
And sometimes a piece of lead is applied, and sometimes a protrusion appears on the back vertebra of the spine, and it is believed to be a dislocation.  

et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:  
But it is the bone that is visible, and no assumption should be made.  

par aventure feroit venir la mort.  
By chance, it could lead to death.  

des dislocations de la hainche  
Of the dislocations of the hip  

Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;  
Know that at the joints of the hip and the shoulder, only dislocations occur, not as with other joints.  

et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:  
And the hip joint can be dislocated in four directions:  

dedens et defuer, et devant et derrier;  
Inward, outward, forward, and backward.  

et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.  
More often inward than elsewhere, and rarely forward or backward.  

Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;  
The sign of an inward dislocation is that when the injured leg is compared with the healthy one, it appears longer, and the knee of the injured leg protrudes more than the healthy one, and the patient cannot bend the knee toward the fire.  

et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.  
And the area nearby is swollen with a hot abscess because the head of the thighbone presses there.  

Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.  
The sign of an outward dislocation is that these symptoms are the opposite of the previous ones.  

Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;  
The sign of a forward dislocation is that the patient can extend the leg completely.  

toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.  
However, they cannot bend the knee without pain, and if they try to walk, they cannot move forward, retain their urine, the groin swells, and when they walk, they step on the heel.  

Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.  
The sign of a backward dislocation is that the patient cannot extend or bend the knee, and that leg is more twisted than the other, the groin is soft, and the head of the thighbone is under the ribs.  

Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;  
The remedy for this type of dislocation is to see if the dislocation is old, and if it remains in its position, there is no treatment.  

et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.  
And no assumptions should be made about it.  

Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;  
But if the dislocation is recent and one of the four types, act quickly to rotate the joint, stretch it inward and outward, and move it to the right and left.  

par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.  
By chance, it will return, and no further treatment is needed.  

Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;  
And if it does not return in this way, it is necessary to prepare a strong assistant, who will stretch the leg strongly with both hands or with a strap tied above the knee.  

et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;  
Another assistant should stretch their hand over in such a way that they place their hands under the armpits and bind the thigh softly with a strap.  

et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;  
And another holds the end of the strap.  

et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.  
And they all stretch upward and downward at the same time until the patient is lifted off the ground all at once and remains suspended.  

Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.  
This method of stretching is common to all four types, and if the dislocation is corrected, as we have said, that is good.  

Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.  
If not, further treatment is required for its type.  

Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;  
When the dislocation is inward, you must place the patient on their healthy side, then place the strap at the root of the thigh and the area beneath the groin, then stretch the strap upward toward the groin and the flank.  

puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:  
Then another assistant should use their arms to brace the thick part of the injured thigh and stretch it outward strongly.  

si revenra a son leu maintenant;  
It will then return to its place immediately.  

et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.  
And this type of dislocation is easier to treat than the others.  

Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;  
And if you cannot set it in the manner we have described, you must bind the two feet of the patient together with a strong, gentle band over the two heels and the two knees, and the injured leg must be stretched two fingers more than the other.

puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;  
Then he should be suspended from the top of a post, two arms' lengths above the ground.

puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.  
Then command one assistant to grasp the top of the thigh, and another assistant, hanging with the patient, should firmly hold the thigh, for the joint will promptly return to its place.

Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;  
And when the dislocation is external, let the patient lie down as we have described for one who is hunchbacked, and tighten a band properly over the injured leg and over the foot as well.

puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;  
Then place two logs, one at the head and the other at the feet, and fix one log between the thighs of the patient, at the center of the body.

et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.  
And wrap damp cloths around it so that the patient is not harmed, then let each assistant pull towards himself, and let the physician adjust the dislocation with his hands.

S’elle revient, c’est boin.  
If it returns, that is good.

Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.  
If not, place him on a table and press as we have described for the hunchback, and let the patient lie on his healthy side.

Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;  
And when the dislocation is forward, the injured leg must be stretched quickly, as I have said.

et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.  
And let the physician exert pressure on the injured hip with one hand, and press with the other hand, extending it downwards towards the knee.

Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;  
And if the dislocation is external, the patient must not be stretched downward or lifted off the ground, but rather positioned as if the hip were dislocated externally, as we have described for lying on both hips.

et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;  
And let him lie on his stomach, with the band extended as we have said before, and pressure must be applied to the joint on the table.

et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;  
And it will be proper when the patient stretches his legs, and they are even.

adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;  
Then align the thighs, apply a plaster, and wrap it with a bandage so that the hip does not move.

et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;  
And let him rest for three or four days, then loosen the bandage and reapply the plaster.

et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;  
And if you see that they are even, rewrap it as before, and leave it for three days.

puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.  
Then loosen it, and let him walk gently, until the limb is strengthened.

de la dislocation dou genoil  
Concerning the dislocation of the knee.

Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:  
The knee is dislocated in three ways:

c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;  
That is, inward, outward, and backward.

et ne desalue point devant.  
And it is not dislocated forward.

Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;  
And the sign is that you command the patient to bend his leg to his thigh, and if it does not press against his thigh, know that it is dislocated.

et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;  
And the restoration for all is that you make the patient sit upright, stretch his leg if he can, place your back against his face, and put his foot on your feet.

puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;  
Then take his knee in your palms, pull it between your fingers, and firmly bend both sides of the knee.

et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;  
And let another assistant extend his foot until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that his leg presses well against his thigh easily.

et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;  
And apply the plaster, make the leg press against the thigh, and bind them tightly together for three or four days, then loosen it.

et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.  
And the patient should not exert himself by walking until the limb is strengthened.

Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
And if the limb is not in place, apply strong stretching, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.

de la dislocation dou talon  
Concerning the dislocation of the heel.

Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.  
The heel is sometimes displaced and sometimes fully dislocated, either inward or outward.

Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:  
And the sign is that the ankle is swollen and projects towards the side where it is dislocated.

li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.  
The reduction is simple, and it must be gently stretched by hand if it is only displaced.

Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;  
And when it is fully dislocated, you must make the patient sit upright, and have one assistant hold the leg firmly above the ankle.  

puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;  
Then pull the foot toward you with your right hand, then with your left hand twice, then extend it upward and gently push the foot upward.  

et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;  
And do this twice, as we have said, both pushing and pulling the foot.  

s’elle revient, c’est bien;  
If it returns to place, that is good.  

se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;  
If not, begin the process again, for it will return.  

et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;  
And if it cannot return this way, make the patient lie on his back on the ground, and fix a stake firmly into the ground between his thighs, wrapping it with cloths so that it does not injure the patient.  

puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;  
Then let one assistant hold the thigh, and another assistant stretch the foot with his hands or with a band tied over the ankle.  

puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;  
Then let each assistant pull evenly, and the stake should remain between the patient’s thighs to hold him steady during the stretching.  

puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.  
Then let the physician adjust the dislocation with his hands, and another assistant hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will quickly return to place.  

Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;  
And when it is in place, apply the plaster and stuffing, bind it tightly, and tie the foot to the leg, being careful that the nerves behind the ankle are not compressed too tightly.  

puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;  
Then leave it for two or three days, and if the band loosens, rebind it.  

puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;  
Then loosen it on the third or fourth day, and forbid the patient from walking for four days.  

et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.  
And if he walks before this time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.  

Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
And if a hot swelling appears, you must calm it, as we have described elsewhere, until it is healed.  

des dois  
Concerning the fingers.  

Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.  
When the fingers are dislocated, they must be gently stretched without force, and this is an easy matter.  

Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;  
And if the dislocation is in any joint of the back of the foot, you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or a table upright, place your foot on what is visible of the joint, then press firmly with your foot until it returns to place.  

et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;  
And when it is aligned and nothing is apparent, place a two-sided board under the sole of the foot, then bind it tightly, leave it for three days, then loosen it.  

et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.  
And let it rest until it is healed.  

de plaie et de dislocation ensamble  
Concerning wounds and dislocation together.  

Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:  
When a wound accompanies a dislocation and one attempts to treat it, it often happens that the patient dies.  

si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;  
Thus, do not be presumptuous in treatment if you are not skilled in the art, have not practiced it long, and are not compassionate, merciful, and patient, but rather cautious.  

et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;  
And at first, use soothing remedies for hot swelling, and leave the patient in the hands of God if you see no hope of healing.  

et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;  
And when you see hope, then promptly restore the limb to its place before the hot swelling occurs.  

et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;  
And when the limb is in place, apply soothing remedies for hot swelling, and treat the wound as necessary with drying ointments.  

et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;  
And if there is a fracture or small loose bones along with the dislocation, remove them and do what we have said for simple injuries.  

et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.  
And beware of acting out of fear, as I have said, for this will benefit you according to your Creator and for the safety of your soul and your body.
